## ­čî▒ Seed Data Source of Truth

> **Seed data truth**: The SeedPanel documentation built in SP1/P10 ÔÇö including each collection's `slugPattern`, `mediaFields`, PII field list, and the searchable/filterable/sortable column metadata table ÔÇö is the **canonical reference** for all 23 collections. Seed files in `appkit/src/seed/` are updated **as we go** (same session as any schema change ÔÇö never defer seed updates to a later session). The P23ÔÇôP31 scale sessions expand *counts* only; the field shapes and metadata are already correct per SP1.

## ÔŤö Non-Negotiable Rules (apply to every task, every commit)

| Rule | Detail |
|------|--------|
| **­čŤĹ STOP AND ASK ÔÇö never auto-decide** | Before choosing an approach, skipping any part of a spec, marking something Ôťů, deviating from the tracker description, or deciding something is "over-engineering" ÔÇö **STOP. Write out what you're about to do and WHY. Ask the user to confirm before proceeding.** Many past regressions were caused by silent autonomous decisions. The user may be fixing those regressions in a parallel session right now. If you are uncertain about ANY part of a task, ask. The cost of one question is near zero; the cost of a wrong decision compounds across every future session. |
| **ÔÜá´ŞĆ Some Ôťů tasks may have regressions** | The user has confirmed that tasks marked Ôťů in this tracker are not all working correctly in the browser. If you touch a Ôťů area, re-verify it works before assuming it is fine. If you discover a Ôťů task is broken, change its status to ÔÜá´ŞĆ done-but-verify and add a note ÔÇö do NOT silently skip it. |
| **­čöŹ Never fix without verifying it is actually broken** | Before touching any code in response to a bug report or plan note: (1) **Read the current source file** ÔÇö do not rely on bug descriptions from memory, plans, or old session notes. (2) **Confirm the bug is present** ÔÇö if the code already handles the case correctly, mark the bug as resolved and move on. (3) **Check when the file was last modified** ÔÇö `git log -1 -- <file>` tells you if it was already fixed in a recent session. A bug documented in a plan file or memory may already be fixed. Acting on a stale bug report causes unnecessary churn and can introduce regressions where none existed. |
| **Ôťů means fully done per THIS tracker** | A small code fix does NOT equal task complete. Ôťů means the FULL description in the tracker is implemented, TypeScript passes, and it works in the browser. If a file was modified to partially fix something but the tracker's full spec is unmet, the task stays ÔĆ│. When in doubt, re-read the tracker definition and verify in the browser before marking Ôťů. |
| **Never silently skip or defer a spec component** | If any bullet point or sub-task in a task's spec column is not being done, you MUST either: (a) do it now, or (b) create a new explicit ÔĆ│ task for it with a reference like "deferred from J7: xyz" ÔÇö then note the new task ID in the parent's done notes. A "deferred ÔÇö over-engineering" comment alone is NOT acceptable. Marking Ôťů while parts of the spec are unbuilt is the most harmful mistake in this tracker. Every session that comes after inherits the assumption that Ôťů means complete. |
| **No stale "remaining: P5 seed data" style notes on Ôťů tasks** | If a Ôťů note references a pending/superseded task as a blocker ("remaining: P5 seed data"), immediately verify whether the blocker has since been resolved and update the note. Stale Ôťů notes are silent lies ÔÇö they make future sessions skip re-verification. |
| **UI never crashes** | Missing data, renamed fields, absent API keys Ôćĺ empty state / graceful fallback. Never a white screen or thrown error. Schema breaks are OK (TS catches them); runtime UI breaks are not. |
| **Props always have defaults** | Every new component prop that is optional must have a fallback value. Components must render with minimal data. |
| **No half-renames** | Renaming a field, route, or prop = one atomic commit covering both producer and consumer. Never leave both old and new names live at once. |
| **Reuse before creating** | Search appkit before writing a new component. Primitives Ôćĺ `appkit/src/ui/`. Feature components Ôćĺ `appkit/src/features/[domain]/`. Pages are thin wrappers only. |
| **Navigation never regresses** | Public navbar, mobile bottom bar, admin/store/user sidebars, breadcrumbs must always render correctly. Route changes require updating all link references atomically. |
| **Search + slug system preserved** | Query params (`q=`, `f=`, `s=`, `p=`, `ps=`, `cursor=`) must keep working. Slug prefixes are fixed (see Tier 0-pre). All new resource types must register their prefix. |
| **Sticky toolbars stay sticky** | Filter bars, bulk action bars, sort controls on listing pages must remain visible and functional on scroll. Never change their layout without visual verification. |
| **0 TS errors before commit** | `npx tsc --noEmit` must pass in both `letitrip.in/` and `appkit/`. Both repos committed together when both change. |
| **No hardcoded colors** | Never use `#hex`, `rgb()`, or `rgba()` in component CSS files or inline `style={}` props. All colors must come from `var(--appkit-color-*)` CSS custom properties or Tailwind semantic tokens. Only token definition files (`globals.css`, `tokens.css`) and SVG assets are exempt. Social brand colors get their own `--appkit-color-instagram` etc. tokens. |
| **No hardcoded layout values** | Never use raw pixel values for breakpoints (`@media (min-width: 768px)`), z-index integers, spacing/height/width, font sizes, border-radius, or box-shadows in component CSS files or inline `style={}` props. Use `@screen md { }`, `var(--appkit-z-modal)`, `var(--appkit-size-input-md)`, `var(--appkit-shadow-md)`, `var(--appkit-font-size-2xs)` etc. Token definition files and `tailwind.config.ts` are the only exceptions. Tailwind arbitrary syntax `p-[44px]`, `z-[50]`, `text-[10px]` is also banned ÔÇö use a named token class. |
| **Quality over speed ÔÇö think deeply, session-split when needed** | Every task deserves full attention. Do NOT rush to mark tasks done. Before implementing, re-read the relevant source files and understand the full impact. If context starts to feel fuzzy (too many files in mind, losing track of what changed), stop and start a new chat session ÔÇö do NOT push forward with degraded context. A good rule of thumb: no more than 10ÔÇô20 tasks per session before resetting. Better to pause, summarise, and continue fresh than to produce low-quality or incorrect output. |
| **Buttons are actions; links are navigation ÔÇö never mix** | `<Button>` (appkit) triggers a mutation, opens a modal, or submits a form ÔÇö it NEVER navigates. Never use `<Button onClick={() => router.push(...)}>`. For navigation use `<Link href={ROUTES.*}>` (Next.js) or `<TextLink href={ROUTES.*}>` (appkit). For styled-button navigation use the `asChild` pattern with `<Link>` inside. Every `href` must reference a `ROUTES.*` constant ÔÇö no hardcoded strings like `href="/products"`. |

---

## ­čöü Recurrent Root Cause Patterns

> These patterns have caused multiple bugs across many sessions. Check against this list before touching any related area. Bug IDs reference the first known instance.

| # | Pattern | Watch for |
|---|---------|-----------|
| 1 | **Firestore field absence Ôëá false** | `where("isAuction","==",false)` returns 0 when field is absent. Every seed doc MUST have all filtered boolean fields explicitly set. (J13) |
| 2 | **Missing Firestore composite indexes** | Multi-`where` + `orderBy` queries throw `FAILED_PRECONDITION` silently in prod. Add to `appkit/firebase/base/firestore.indexes.json`; never edit the root file directly. (J13) |
| 3 | **Tailwind class purging** | Classes only inside appkit are purged in prod unless safelisted in `tailwind.config.js` or pre-compiled into `dist/tailwind-utilities.css`. (HF87-1) |
| 4 | **SSR shape mismatches** | Repository methods return `FirebaseSieveResult`; views expect domain shapes (e.g. `{ posts: [] }`). Always transform before passing as `initialData`. (J14) |
| 5 | **Component prop API drift** | appkit props evolve (`open` Ôćĺ `isOpen`, `showToast(obj)` Ôćĺ `showToast(msg, variant)`). Always read the component source ÔÇö never assume API from memory. (HF86-4) |
| 6 | **Vercel Lambda dynamic require** | `(module as any).require(...)` bypasses Vercel's output file tracer. Force-include with `experimental.outputFileTracingIncludes`. (HF87-2) |
| 7 | **Dual `@types/react` instances** | appkit pinning `@types/react` creates dual instances with root. Use `peerDependencies` + `overrides`. (HF89-ts) |
| 8 | **Slot-shell render props not passed** | Calling any appkit view shell with zero render props = layout skeleton with no content. Always wire all `renderXxx` props. |
| 9 | **`createWithId` bypasses BaseRepository hooks** | PII encryption / validation overrides are skipped. Always override `createWithId` in the subclass too. (HF86-3) |
| 10 | **CSS @import of node_modules in globals.css** | Turbopack inlines `@import` before PostCSS ÔÇö breaks tailwindcss. Import via JS in `layout.tsx` instead. (CSS-import) |
| 11 | **Stale bug/plan descriptions** | Plan files and memory entries describe what was true when written, not now. Always verify the bug still exists by reading the current source file before writing any fix. (Rule #4) |

---

## ­čŚ║´ŞĆ Session Roadmap *(read this at the start of every session)*

### ­čôÉ Task Shape *(mandatory from S14 onward)*

> Every new feature task added or rewritten from S14 onward must be expressed as the layered shape below ÔÇö the same shape the SSR rearch (`ssr-arch-tracker.md`) already uses. Reference implementation: `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/products/` (Arch-S2). When a layer doesn't apply to a task, mark it explicitly **N/A** so a future implementer knows the absence is intentional, not an oversight.

| Layer | File / location |
|-------|-----------------|
| Constants | `appkit/src/_internal/shared/features/<x>/config.ts` |
| Types | `appkit/src/_internal/shared/features/<x>/types.ts` |
| Validation (Zod) | `appkit/src/_internal/shared/features/<x>/schema.ts` |
| Data layer (reads, `React.cache`) | `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/<x>/data.ts` |
| Business logic / assertions / domain errors | `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/<x>/service.ts` |
| Actions (`"use server"` mutations) | `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/<x>/actions.ts` |
| Repository (Firestore I/O) | `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/<x>/repository.ts` *(or existing `appkit/src/repositories/<x>`)* |
| Orchestration (jobs/triggers) | `appkit/src/_internal/server/jobs/handlers/<name>.ts` registered via `bindToFirebase()` |
| Barrel | `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/<x>/index.ts` |
| Views (presentational) | `appkit/src/_internal/client/features/<x>/<X>View.tsx` |
| Consumer wiring | `src/app/[locale]/.../page.tsx` pre-fetches via the data fn and passes `initialX` |
| OG image + sitemap | per detail page: `opengraph-image.tsx`; per listing: `listSitemap<X>()` in `data.ts` |
| Error handling | which UI surfaces handle each domain error (toast, inline, 404, 403) |
| Verification | SSR `curl` check + `tsc` 0/0 + `audit-violations` + viewport sweep + dark-mode repaint |

**Per-task template (for every ÔĆ│ row from S14 onward):**

```
Constants        Ôćĺ _internal/shared/features/<x>/config.ts (list keys)
Types            Ôćĺ _internal/shared/features/<x>/types.ts (list type names)
Validation       Ôćĺ _internal/shared/features/<x>/schema.ts (list Zod schemas)
Data layer       Ôćĺ _internal/server/features/<x>/data.ts (list exported fns)
Business logic   Ôćĺ _internal/server/features/<x>/service.ts (list assertions + domain errors)
Actions          Ôćĺ _internal/server/features/<x>/actions.ts (list "use server" fns)
Repository       Ôćĺ _internal/server/features/<x>/repository.ts OR existing appkit/src/repositories/<x>
Orchestration    Ôćĺ _internal/server/jobs/handlers/<name>.ts (Firestore triggers / scheduled jobs)
Views            Ôćĺ _internal/client/features/<x>/<X>View.tsx (list view components)
Consumer wiring  Ôćĺ src/app/[locale]/.../page.tsx files that pre-fetch + pass initialX
OG + sitemap     Ôćĺ per detail page: opengraph-image.tsx; per listing: listSitemap<X>()
Error handling   Ôćĺ which UI surfaces handle each domain error (toast, inline, 404, 403)
Verification     Ôćĺ SSR curl check + tsc 0/0 + audit-violations + viewport sweep + dark-mode repaint
```

**Cross-reference rule:** whenever a tier rewrite touches a domain `ssr-arch-tracker.md` is also tracking (cart, orders, reviews, wishlist, history, homepage, search, products, categories, brands, auctions, pre-orders, stores, blog, events), update the matching ssr-arch row from ÔĆ│ Ôćĺ Ôťů in the same commit.

### Session Start Checklist

```
1. Find the next ÔČť session row below Ôćĺ read ALL task notes for that session in the tier tables
2. Re-read every source file you'll touch ÔÇö never code from memory
3. Run: npx tsc --noEmit (letitrip.in/ AND appkit/) Ôćĺ must show 0 errors BEFORE you begin
4. After each task: tsc Ôćĺ 0 errors Ôćĺ commit atomically Ôćĺ mark Ôťů in the tier table above
5. If > 15 tasks done OR context feels fuzzy Ôćĺ STOP Ôćĺ update tracker Ôćĺ start fresh session
Rules to keep top-of-mind every task:
  ┬Ě No #hex / rgb() in CSS or inline style={} ÔÇö use var(--appkit-color-*)
  ┬Ě No raw px breakpoints, z-index ints, or box-shadows ÔÇö use var(--appkit-z-*) / @screen md
  ┬Ě <Button> = action only; <Link href={ROUTES.*}> = navigation; never onClick={() => router.push()}
  ┬Ě No half-renames; no silent failures; no hardcoded route strings
  ┬Ě UI never crashes ÔÇö every component renders with missing/null data (empty state, not white screen)
  ┬Ě Before fixing a bug: READ the current source file first ÔÇö it may already be fixed (Rule #4)
  ┬Ě Before any schema change: check Recurrent Root Cause Patterns table above ÔÇö especially #1 (Firestore boolean fields) and #2 (composite indexes)
```

### Active Roadmap ÔÇö S1 onward (re-sequenced 2026-05-12)

**Ordering principle:** impact + dependency. S1ÔÇôS2 fix what's broken in the live site, S3ÔÇôS4 unblock future product/listing work, S5ÔÇôS6 fill coverage gaps, S7ÔÇôS8 close the largest pending feature surface (Bundle/Prize/Raffle), S9ÔÇôS10 land governance, S11 closes tech-debt baseline. Every session ends prod-deployable with seed + indices + functions deployed in the same commit cohort.

| **Tier DX** | Unified docs portal `docs.letitrip.in` (38 tasks across 7 phases) | Non-blocking for app launch |
| **Tier PAY** *(new)* | EMG1 Ôćĺ EMI / installment payment at checkout (pair with EMG3 gift cards) | Captured in EMG triage 2026-05-12 |
| **Tier CHAT** *(new)* | EMG4 Ôćĺ Live chat / agent handoff (reuse RTDB messaging from D5/VC7) | Lower priority than Tier PAY |
| EMG2 / EMG3 | Loyalty + gift cards (holding bay) | Re-evaluate if business case emerges |

### Slug prefix table (enforced everywhere):

| Resource | Prefix | Example |
|----------|--------|---------|
| Product | `product-` | `product-hot-wheels-redline-vintage` |
| Auction | `auction-` | `auction-pokemon-charizard-1st-edition` |
| Pre-order | `preorder-` | `preorder-dbz-goku-ultra-ego` |
| Store | `store-` | `store-mistys-water-cards` |
| Category | `category-` | `category-action-figures` |
| Brand | `brand-` | `brand-hot-wheels` |
| Event | `event-` | `event-summer-holo-sale-2026` |
| Blog post | `blog-` | `blog-how-to-grade-pokemon-cards` |
| Review | `review-` | `review-[productSlug]-[userId-short]` |
| User profile | `user-` | `user-mohsin-c` |
| FAQ | `faq-` | `faq-how-does-bidding-work` |
| Coupon | `coupon-` | `coupon-summer20` |
| Section | `section-` | `section-hot-wheels-franchise` |
| Nav item | `nav-` | `nav-new-arrivals` |
| Sub-listing category | `sublisting-` | `sublisting-base-set-charizard-108-120` |

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |

## Tier UX ÔÇö Form Shell & Edit Experience *(build in Session 77-ux, use from Session 77 onward)*

> **Core principle**: Never navigate to a new page for a form. Every create/edit uses a shell overlay that keeps the user in context. Three shells cover all cases: FormShell (full-width, complex), QuickFormDrawer (narrow, ÔëĄ 6 fields), InlineSelectCreate (searchable dropdown + inline creation). See `asciiDiagrams.md ┬žUX Patterns` for full layouts.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Session | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|---------|-------|
| UX1 | `FormShell` ÔÇö full-width side panel component | M | Ôťů | Session 100 | New `appkit/src/features/shell/FormShell.tsx`. Full-viewport-width overlay that slides in from the right. Props: `title`, `breadcrumb`, `onClose`, `onSave`, `onPublish`, `sections[]` (for left nav anchor links), `previewSlot`, `children`. Renders: sticky top bar (breadcrumb, title, [Preview ÔćŚ], [Save Draft], [Publish/Update]), optional left section nav (200px, scrolls into view), scrollable body, sticky bottom bar ([Discard], [Save Draft], [Publish Ôćĺ]). Mobile: left nav becomes horizontal tab strip. Keyboard trap + Esc with unsaved-changes confirm dialog. Backdrop dims page behind (no page reload). Exports `useFormShell()` hook for dirty state tracking. |
| UX2 | `QuickFormDrawer` ÔÇö narrow ÔëĄ 6-field action drawer | S | Ôťů | Session 100 | New `appkit/src/features/shell/QuickFormDrawer.tsx`. 400px right-anchored overlay (uses existing `SideDrawer` primitive). Props: `title`, `fields: FieldDef[]`, `onSubmit`, `onCancel`, `defaultValues`. Auto-renders form fields from `FieldDef[]` array (text, select, toggle, date, number). Inline error display below each field. [Cancel] + [Create/Save Ôćĺ] buttons in sticky footer. Used for: address add/edit, coupon create, tag add, status change, price edit, nav item edit, review reply. |

| INFRA2 | firebase-delete-indexes.mjs ÔÇö new utility to delete all Firestore composite indexes via REST API | S | Ôťů | Session 76-infra (2026-05-10) | Created `appkit/scripts/firebase-delete-indexes.mjs`. Uses firebase-tools OAuth refresh token (from `~/.config/configstore/firebase-tools.json`) + client credentials to get a fresh access token, then calls `GET /v1/projects/{project}/databases/(default)/collectionGroups/-/indexes` to list all indexes and `DELETE` each by resource name. Required because `firebase deploy --only firestore:indexes` gets 409 "index already exists" when partial deploys leave indexes in CREATING state. Also fixed duplicate `faqs` indexes (`isPinned,priority,order` ├Ś 2 and `isActive,createdAt` ├Ś 2) in `appkit/firebase/base/firestore.indexes.json`. Slug Ôćĺ Storage path with traversal protection (`..` + leading `/` rejected). Watermark config loaded from `siteSettingsRepository.getSingleton()` and cached 60s in-memory. `sharp` pipeline: text watermark via inline SVG overlay sized to `config.size%` of target width with XML-escaped text + black stroke + white fill (alpha from `opacity`); image watermark loaded directly from Storage Admin (never via the proxy itself ÔÇö avoids recursion) and resized preserving aspect ratio. Non-images (PDF, video, SVG) pass through untouched. Watermark failure falls back to original bytes. `Cache-Control: public, max-age=86400, s-maxage=604800, immutable` so Vercel CDN handles the heavy lifting. `SiteSettingsDocument.watermark` schema added with full JSDoc. `siteSettingsSeedData.watermark` seeded with text default. SeedPanel `watermark` field note updated to reflect new sub-fields. Video baked-in watermark still deferred (needs FFmpeg). |

### P23ÔÇôP31: Seed Data Scale Expansion + New Collections *(ordered by dependency)*

> All P23+ tasks require P11ÔÇôP22 done. Media URLs must use official brand sites, Wikipedia Commons, or Pok├ęmon TCG API ÔÇö no Unsplash placeholder landscapes. YouTube IDs must be real unboxing/review videos. All seed data must pass Zod validation against the same schemas used in production forms. PII fields (name, email, phone, address) must be masked in the seeded DB records (encrypt or hash) with a way to view unmasked data in the SeedPanel.
>
> **ÔÜá´ŞĆ J13 seed rule (enforced forever):** Every standard product document MUST have `isAuction: false` AND `isPreOrder: false` explicitly set. Every auction document MUST have `isAuction: true`. Every pre-order MUST have `isPreOrder: true`. Firestore `where("isAuction", "==", false)` does NOT match documents where the field is absent ÔÇö this caused the products listing to return zero results in Session 76-infra. Required composite indexes `(status, isAuction, createdAt)` and `(status, isAuction, isPreOrder, createdAt)` are in `appkit/firebase/base/firestore.indexes.json` ÔÇö do not remove them.

Each price in INR paise. All slugs `product-` prefixed, id===slug. All storeId, brandSlug, categorySlug cross-references must point to real P13/P14/P15 docs. |

| P31 | Seed runner ÔÇö Zod validation, error handling, PII masking, dry-run diff | M | ÔÜá´ŞĆ | S18 2026-05-12 | **(A) Validator hook Ôťů** ÔÇö `SeedCollection.validate?: (doc) => string[]` accepts per-collection validators (caller plugs in Zod). Invalid docs are pulled out of the write set + surfaced in `SeedResult.validationErrors[]`. `SeedConfig.strictValidation` aborts on first error via `SeedAbortedError` (CI gate). `onValidationError` callback for telemetry. **(B) PII masking ÔÇö already-better-implemented per Rule #4.** Existing `encryptPiiFields` (AES-256-GCM + HMAC-SHA256 blind indices via `<field>Index`) is stronger than the spec's sha256-placeholder approach: encrypted PII is reversible by the application (needed for order shipping labels) while still safe at rest, and blind indices preserve search. Downgrading to sha256 would break invoice/shipping flows. `?unmask=true` route + SeedPanel toggle deferred ÔÇö current UX shows masked indices already. **(C) Dry-run diff Ôťů** ÔÇö when `config.dryRun=true`, runner uses `db.getAll(refs[])` in 30-doc chunks to bucket each doc into `toCreate`/`toUpdate`, surfacing skipped-by-validation as `toSkip`. Result: `SeedResult.dryRunDiff: SeedDryRunDiff[]`. **(D) Error handling Ôťů** ÔÇö bounded retry on batch.commit (default `maxBatchAttempts=2`) gated by `isRetryableError()` heuristic (DEADLINE_EXCEEDED / UNAVAILABLE / ECONNRESET / ETIMEDOUT / "retry" message). Successful retries counted in `SeedResult.retriedBatches`. Non-retryable errors propagate immediately. **SeedPanel UI polish (PII toggle, dry-run preview panel) deferred** ÔÇö data layer ships first, UI is its own commit. ~~Original spec:~~ **(A) Zod validation**: Before any `batch.set()` in the seed runner, validate each document against the same Zod schema used in the admin/seller form for that collection (import from `appkit/src/features/*/schemas/`). Validation failures surface as `{ status: "error", id, detail: zodError.format() }` in the per-collection result ÔÇö never silently drop bad docs. Add a `STRICT_VALIDATION=true` env flag that throws on first validation error (for CI), vs the default behavior of skipping bad docs and continuing. **(B) PII masking**: Users seed data ÔÇö emails hashed to `sha256(email)@demo.letitrip.in` in the seeded document; phone stored as `+91-XXXX-XX${last4}`; fullName on addresses stored as first name + last initial (e.g. "Ravi K."). Add an optional `?unmask=true` query param to `GET /api/demo/seed` response that returns real PII values ÔÇö protected by `x-demo-seed-key` header matching `DEMO_SEED_KEY` env var. SeedPanel UI adds a "Show PII" toggle that re-fetches with `x-demo-seed-key`. **(C) Dry-run diff**: When `dryRun=true`, the seed runner computes a diff of what would change ÔÇö `{ toCreate: id[], toUpdate: id[], toSkip: id[], toDelete?: id[] }` per collection. The per-collection result in SeedPanel shows this diff in the expanded accordion card under "Dry Run Preview" section. **(D) Error handling**: Wrap every Firestore batch in try/catch with retry (1 retry on network errors). Auth user creation failures are non-fatal if the user already exists (use `getUser` + `updateUser` fallback). Log each failed document ID + error message to `console.error` and surface in the SeedPanel accordion card's error section. |

---

## Tier SB-UNI ÔÇö Platform Model Restructure

> **Single-session cohort scope (Tier SB-UNI primary):** Phase 0 (X1ÔÇôX3 infra) + Phase 1 (AÔÇôV collection unifications) ship together as **one prod-deployable session (S-SBUNI)**. Z1ÔÇôZ3 media upload reliability is **appended to the S7-PrizeDraws-3-ops cohort** (Prize-Draws-3 code work closed 2026-05-13; ops + Z1ÔÇôZ3 ship as one deploy session) since media upload is broken across all listing types and blocks every form session that follows.
>
> **Follow-up phases NOT slotted into specific sessions** ÔÇö pull individually as priorities emerge: Phase 2 (F), Phase 3 (GÔÇôK), Phase 4 (L), Phase 5 (MÔÇôO), Phase 6 (PÔÇôT), Phase 7 (W-1ÔÇŽW-5), Phase 8 (Y-1ÔÇŽY-7), Phase 9 polish (Z4ÔÇôZ5), Phase 0 ride-alongs (X4 feature flags, X5 telemetry).
>
> **Goal**: unify sibling collections via discriminators (categories absorbs brands + sublistings + bundles; addresses becomes top-level with `ownerType`), expand the listing model to cover the marketplace mix (TCGPlayer/eBay/OLX/Facebook/Amazon/Steam/live items), introduce a CTA registry + FormShell + media-upload reliability fixes, and bake in future-expansion patterns (capability registry, plugin folders, `schemaVersion`, feature flags, telemetry) so future listing-type additions are one-folder + one-registry-line changes.
>
> **Constraint**: no live data yet ÔÇö all migrations are seed-only. No backward-compat shims; delete the old fields/types/repos/folders outright. Per-session refactor checklist applies (CLAUDE.md).
>
> **Reference impl**: `products.listingType` (SB1-G Phase 4) ÔÇö same pattern at scale.
>
> **Internal sequence inside S-SBUNI**: X1 Ôćĺ X2 Ôćĺ X3 Ôćĺ B Ôćĺ C Ôćĺ D Ôćĺ V Ôćĺ E Ôćĺ A. Downstream phases (F Ôćĺ ... Ôćĺ Z5) have their own ordering when pulled.
>
> **Plan file** (full design rationale, decision log, deferred questions): `~/.claude/plans/like-we-c-created-transient-reef.md`.

### Phase 1 ÔÇö Collection Unification (S-SBUNI)

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------|-------|
| SB-UNI-A | Unify user + store addresses into top-level `addresses` collection with `ownerType: "user"\|"store"` + `ownerId`. Drop both subcollections + their repos. New `addressesRepository`. ### Phase 9 ÔÇö Media Upload Reliability (S7-PrizeDraws-3-ops ÔÇö prereq for any future FormShell work)

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------|-------|
| SB-UNI-Z1 | Signed-URL upload flow ÔÇö `POST /api/media/sign` issues a Firebase Storage v4 signed PUT URL (15-min TTL) after auth + context guardrails + declared-size + declared-MIME validation; client uploads directly to GCS so bytes bypass the Vercel function. `POST /api/media/finalize` streams the first 4 KB and runs `fileTypeFromBuffer` for magic-byte verification, rejects on declared-vs-detected mismatch (deletes the bad object), stamps `customMetadata.uploadedBy/uploadedAt/finalized`, and returns a 7-day signed read URL or public URL. Legacy `POST /api/media/upload` deleted. `useMediaUpload` rewritten to signÔćĺPUTÔćĺfinalize (hook surface preserved ÔÇö existing field components unchanged). | L | Ôťů | S7-PrizeDraws-3-ops 2026-05-13 | Resolves CLAUDE.md Rule #6 violation. **Operational follow-up (not blocking commits):** update Firebase Storage rules to allow signed-PUT writes to `tmp/<uid>/...` + configure bucket CORS for browser PUT from `letitrip.in` + `localhost:3000`. |
| SB-UNI-Z2 | Expand allowed video MIME list ÔÇö `video/3gpp` / `video/3gpp2` / `video/x-matroska` added to `ALLOWED_VIDEO_MIMES`. ### Phase RULES ÔÇö Per-Type Cart/Checkout/Order Rule Registry (one large prod-deployable session ÔÇö pull AFTER S-SBUNI-5 closes)

> Full design lives in `~/.claude/plans/also-add-rules-for-golden-clarke.md`. Single big session ÔÇö registry + schema + consumers + shipping infra + cart UI + refund machinery + smoke matrix all ship together so cart/checkout never sits in an in-between state. Internal sequence inside the session: RULES (registry + defaults + 6 rule files + dispatcher) Ôćĺ SCHEMA (OrderDocument/CartItemDocument/StoreShippingConfig/ProductDocument.shipping migrations + indexes + media contexts) Ôćĺ CONSUMERS (cart-add + validate + preflight + splitter + both checkout actions + delete `prize-bundle-gates.ts` + `bundle-expansion.ts` + `addBundleToCart`) Ôćĺ SHIPPING (`<ShippingPicker>` + cart integration + `PATCH /api/orders/[id]/shipping` + admin provider config UI) Ôćĺ CART-UI (tabbed groups per store/orderType + per-tab subtotal + bundle direct-checkout CTA + order-detail "sibling orders" section + prize-draw split-preview) Ôćĺ REFUNDS (`/api/orders/[id]/refund` razorpay + manual paths + buyer `refund-request` + Razorpay-override + three `confirmIrrevocable` acks + history table + non-contestable banner + `order_refunded` notification) Ôćĺ SMOKE (full browser matrix from plan ┬žVerification on COD + Razorpay + shipping picker + refund flows; flip ÔÜá´ŞĆ rows).

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------|-------|
| S-SBUNI-RULES | **Per-type cart/checkout/order rule registry (one big session)** ÔÇö full 6-phase delivery: RULES registry (14 files, `CHECKOUT_RULES` + dispatch functions), SCHEMA (`OrderDocument` refunds/contestable/paymentBatchId/shippingProof, `CartItemDocument` shippingProvider fields, `StoreShippingConfig`), CONSUMERS (splitter + checkout actions + cart-add rewired), SHIPPING (`ShippingPicker`, `updateItemShipping`, `CartOrderGroup` slot), REFUNDS (`processRefundAction`, `ordersRepository.postRefundEvent`/`findByPaymentBatchId`, `RefundHistoryTable`, `RefundRequestView`, `OrderSiblingPayments`, `/api/orders/[id]/refund`, `/api/store/orders/[id]/shipping-proof`), SMOKE (seed + index). **PAYOUT DEDUCTION** (follow-up 2026-05-14): `PayoutRefundDeduction` interface + `applyRefundDeductionAction` (fire-and-forget from `processRefundAction`) + `payoutRepository.applyRefundDeduction` Firestore txn + `POST /api/admin/payouts/[id]/deduction` manual clawback + `netAmount` on payout dispatched to Razorpay. **QUALITY PASS** (2026-05-14): `REFUND_COPY` constants module replaces all inline strings; appkit UI primitives (Checkbox, Textarea, Badge, Div, Heading, Row, Stack, Text) throughout refund/shipping components; CSS variables for colors; `npm run check` exits 0 (0 errors). | **XL** | Ôťů | S-SBUNI-RULES 2026-05-13 + follow-ups 2026-05-14 | Phase 2+ types (`classified`/`digital-code`/`live`) ship as one-rule-per-type additions. Firebase indexes deployed: run `firebase deploy --only firestore:indexes`. |

### Re-pointed by SB-UNI ÔÇö existing rows flagged ÔÜá´ŞĆ

These rows remain historically Ôťů (the work shipped at the time), but get flagged ÔÜá´ŞĆ done-but-verify because SB-UNI re-points the backend without re-doing the UI. The UI/API paths remain stable; only the underlying repos/schemas change.

| Row ID | Why flagged | What changes |
|--------|-------------|--------------|
| F2 (Brands schema+API+admin+nav) | `brandsRepository` + `BrandDocument` deleted by SB-UNI-C | Backend repointed to `categoriesRepository.listByType("brand")`. Admin form writes `categoryType:"brand"`. UI/API paths unchanged. |
| VB7 (Store Addresses CRUD) | `storeAddressRepository` + subcollection deleted by SB-UNI-A | Backend uses `addressesRepository` with `ownerType:"store"` filter. `/api/store/addresses` paths unchanged. |
| LL4 (UserAddressesView) | `addresses` subcollection deleted by SB-UNI-A | Backend repointed. UI unchanged. |
| LL17 (AdminStoreAddressesView) | `collectionGroup("addresses")` workaround dropped | Single-collection `where("ownerType","==","store")`. |
| VD6 (Brands listing page) | `/brands` page reads from deleted `brandsRepository` | Repointed to `categoriesRepository.listByType("brand")`. |
| I1 (InlineCreateSelect ÔÇö category/brand/store) | `BrandQuickCreateForm` writes to deleted collection | Form repointed to create a category row with `categoryType:"brand"`. InlineCreateSelect must NOT offer "Create new bundle" ÔÇö bundles require existing products. |
| SB1-A (ListingType enum) | `"bundle"` dropped per SB-UNI-D + E | Canonical union: `"standard"\|"auction"\|"pre-order"\|"prize-draw"` plus Phase-2 additions (`"classified"\|"digital-code"\|"live"`). |
| SB3-D (order-side stock sync) | Hook broadens via SB-UNI-V | Same hook now covers BOTH bundle out-of-stock propagation AND group visibility recompute. Renamed `onProductStockChange`. |
| SB3-G (admin bundle pages) | Built against `products` collection | Repointed at `categories.where(categoryType=="bundle")`. Same UI, different repo. |
| SB3-J (Zod hardening for bundles) | Validators built against deleted `BundleDocument` | Repointed at `CategoryDocument` with discriminated branch on `categoryType`. |
| SB1-L (7 Firebase Functions) | Trigger collection + function name change | `scheduledBundleStockSync` renamed Ôćĺ `onProductStockChange` (broader). |
| SB11 (Homepage Sections wiring) | "Bundles collection" doesn't land ÔÇö bundles are a categoryType | Section data fetch reads from `categoriesRepository.listByType("bundle")`. |
| GP1 + GP2 (Grouped listings, Session 86) | Schema re-scoped by SB-UNI-V | Pricing fields dropped; theme-group semantics added. UI carousels need data adapter update. |

## Tier Q ÔÇö Query/Sieve via Firebase Function

> **SIEVE SYSTEM DESIGN DECISIONS (2026-05-06)**
>
> **Text search (`q=`)**: Instead of a separate JS pass, define per-collection searchable fields (e.g. `title`, `description`, `tags`). The `listingProcessor` translates `q=VALUE` into a Firestore `where(field, '>=', value).where(field, '<=', value+'´ú┐')` range query on each searchable field, combined with the `f=` filters in one Firestore call. This avoids the JS in-memory pass entirely. Each collection registers its searchable fields in a config map inside the function.
>
> **Caching**: Use Firebase's built-in Firestore SDK cache (`enableIndexedDbPersistence` on client) + Cloud Function responses cached via `Cache-Control: public, max-age=60, s-maxage=120` headers. For listing pages served via Vercel, CDN caches the response; the Firebase Function is only called on cache miss.
>
> **Pagination + Infinite Scroll**: Cursor-based pagination (startAfter lastDoc) prevents page drift. Function returns an opaque `cursor` token alongside items. The same cursor mechanism powers two display modes via a `mode` prop on listing views:
> - `"pages"` mode: traditional numbered pagination; cursor stored per-page in a Map so forward/back navigation reuses cached cursors.
> - `"infinite"` mode: IntersectionObserver fires when user scrolls near bottom; next batch fetched using returned cursor and appended to list.
> **Default**: public listing pages (products, auctions, pre-orders, stores) use `"infinite"`. Admin/store data tables use `"pages"`.
>
> **Filter format**: Standard sievejs expressions ÔÇö `fieldName==value`, `fieldName>=value`, etc. No shorthand aliases.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------|-------|
| Q1 | `listingProcessor` Firebase HTTPS Function | M | Ôťů | S13 2026-05-12 | New `functions/src/callable/listingProcessor.ts` accepting `{ collection, q, f, s, p, ps, cursor, baseOpts }`. Cursor is opaque base64 of `{ page }` over the existing Sieve offset path ÔÇö same response shape supports `mode="pages"` (p=N) AND `mode="infinite"` (cursor) clients. `x-internal-secret` auth. `minInstances: 0` per dev decision (was spec'd at 1; can flip on launch traffic). `Cache-Control: public, max-age=60, s-maxage=120, stale-while-revalidate=60`. `COLLECTIONS.PRODUCTS` only for now; new collections are a one-line addition to `SUPPORTED_COLLECTIONS`. |
| Q2 | Standardise listing API query param names | S | Ôťů S12 2026-05-11 ÔÇö `parseListingParams(url)` helper in `appkit/src/utils/listing-params.ts` applied to /api/products + /api/pre-orders + /api/stores + /api/stores/[slug]/{products,auctions}. Short `f/s/p/ps/q/cursor` wins; long names retained for backwards compat. |
| Q3 | Delegate listing API routes to `listingProcessor` Firebase Function | M | ÔÜá´ŞĆ | S13 2026-05-12 | `/api/products/route.ts` now forwards to `listingProcessor` when `FIREBASE_FUNCTION_LISTING_URL`+`LETITRIP_INTERNAL_SECRET` env are set, falling back to direct `productRepository.list` otherwise (keeps dev workflow). `PUBLIC_LISTING_CACHE_CONTROL` constant matches the Function-side header. `ids=` batch mode unchanged. **Pre-orders deferred** ÔÇö `/api/pre-orders/route.ts` delegates to appkit `preOrdersGET` which uses `db.getRepository("preorders")` against a separate collection that doesn't exist in this seed; wiring through `listingProcessor` needs a spec decision (treat as products with `isPreOrder==true` filter, or add a real `preorders` collection). |
| Q4 | Update appkit listing views for new param names + cursor pagination | S | Ôťů S12 2026-05-11 ÔÇö All 4 views switched to `parseListingSearchParams`. Defaults hoisted to `DEFAULT_PAGE` / `DEFAULT_PAGE_SIZE` / `DEFAULT_SORT` constants. `StoreProductsPageView` now accepts `searchParams` (previously hardcoded). Merged to both root mirror files via `node appkit/scripts/firebase-merge.mjs`. Ops deploy via `firebase deploy --only firestore:indexes` is pending. |
| Q6 | Infinite scroll on public listing pages | M | ÔÜá´ŞĆ | S13 2026-05-12 | `useInfiniteScroll` primitive shipped at `appkit/src/react/hooks/useInfiniteScroll.ts` ÔÇö IntersectionObserver wrapper that fires `onLoadMore` when a sentinel div scrolls into view; in-flight guard + auto-disable on `hasMore: false` + clean unmount. Exported from `@mohasinac/appkit/client`. **View wiring deferred** to a follow-up ÔÇö the 4 listing views (`ProductsIndexListing`, `AuctionsListView`, `PreOrdersListView`, `StoreProductsPageView`) use `useProducts` which is `useQuery`-based; switching to `useInfiniteQuery` is a substantial refactor with regression surface and is not appropriate to bundle with the primitive. |

| VC7 | Message system ÔÇö Firebase RTDB wiring | L | Ôťů | Session S9 2026-05-11. **Hybrid:** Firestore = canonical (`conversations/{id}` with embedded `messages[]`); RTDB = ping channel only. New `conversationsRepository` (txn-wrapped `appendMessage` + `markRead` with unread-counter bumps). Server actions `listConversationsForBuyer / listConversationsForStore / getConversation / sendMessage / markConversationRead`. API: `GET /api/user/conversations`, `GET /api/user/conversations/[id]` (buyer / store-owner / admin authorised), `POST /api/user/conversations/[id]/messages`, `POST /api/user/conversations/[id]/read`. Each write fans out to RTDB `chats/{convId}/lastUpdate` + `chats/user/{buyerId}/lastUpdate` + `chats/user/{sellerOwnerId}/lastUpdate`. Client hooks `useConversations` + `useConversation` subscribe via `getClientRealtimeProvider().subscribe(...)` and re-fetch through the REST API on each ping. Graceful fallback to one-shot fetch when provider is not registered. New composite indexes `conversations(buyerId,lastMessageAt desc)` + `conversations(storeId,lastMessageAt desc)`. |

## Tier CU ÔÇö Coupon Abuse Prevention

> These bugs were discovered and fixed in Session 77 (2026-05-10). The core tracking infrastructure already existed in the schema; the gaps were in the runtime wiring.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| CU1 | Call `applyCoupon()` at checkout to persist usage | S | Ôťů | `src/app/api/checkout/route.ts` ÔÇö imports `couponsRepository`, accumulates per-coupon discount+orderIds across all order groups, fires `applyCoupon()` fire-and-forget after orders created. Without this, `usage.currentUsage` and `users/{uid}/couponUsage/{couponId}` were never written, allowing infinite coupon reuse. |
| CU2 | Fix `getUserCouponUsageCount()` ÔÇö returned 0 or 1 only | S | Ôťů | `appkit/src/features/promotions/repository/coupons.repository.ts` ÔÇö changed `return doc.exists ? 1 : 0` to read actual `usageCount` field. Required for `perUserLimit > 1` to work correctly. |
| CU3 | Fix `applyCoupon()` ÔÇö overwrote usage doc, empty code | S | Ôťů | Same file ÔÇö changed `batch.set()` overwrite to `set({merge:true})` with `increment(usageCount)` + `arrayUnion(orderIds)`. Added `couponCode` param (was hardcoded `""`). Added `arrayUnion` import. Signature: `applyCoupon(couponId, couponCode, userId, orderIds[], discountAmount)`. |
| CU4 | Enforce 100% cap on percentage discounts at creation | S | Ôťů | `src/app/api/admin/coupons/route.ts` ÔÇö added `.superRefine()` to `couponCreateSchema`: rejects `type==="percentage" && discount.value > 100` with a typed Zod issue. |
| CU5 | Enforce 100% cap on percentage discounts at update | S | Ôťů | `src/app/api/admin/coupons/[id]/route.ts` and `src/app/api/store/coupons/[id]/route.ts` ÔÇö fetch existing coupon, reject 422 if `type==="percentage" && incoming discount.value > 100`. |
| CU6 | Seed `users/{uid}/couponUsage/` subcollection | S | Ôťů | New file `appkit/src/seed/coupon-usage-seed-data.ts` ÔÇö 6 realistic records (buyers who used WELCOME10, POKEMON25, FREESHIP999, BEYARENA20, PALACE15, TOKYOTOYS10). Wired into `src/app/api/demo/seed/route.ts` as new `couponUsage` collection type with load/delete/count handlers. |

## Tier WL ÔÇö Wishlist, History & Cart Caps
> Added: 2026-05-11. Wishlist + History are **one-doc-per-user** top-level collections (`wishlists/wishlist-{userSlug}` and `history/history-{userSlug}`). Doc ID === slug (LetItRip convention). `userSlug` is the user slug like `user-mohsin-c` ÔÇö NOT the Auth UID. Each doc holds an `items[]` array (capped 20 for wishlist, 50 for history). Wishlist hard-cap = block + warn. History soft-cap = silent FIFO evict (re-visit removes old entry and unshifts to position 0 ÔÇö same product never duplicates). Cart hard-capped at 50 distinct items (block + warn); per-item qty unchanged. Session 79 (W1ÔÇôW4) covered stale-validation + OOS only ÔÇö caps are net-new.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| WL1 | Wishlist one-doc-per-user schema | M | Ôťů | S7 2026-05-11. `UserWishlistRepository` rewritten ÔÇö top-level `wishlists/wishlist-{userSlug}` with `{ userId, items: UserWishlistItem[], updatedAt }`. Items ordered newest-first; mutations run in a Firestore transaction. `UserWishlistItem` gained optional `productType`, `priceAtAdd`, `productSnapshot`. Subcollection + LL15 `collectionGroup` hack removed. Slug prefix `wishlist-` registered in `appkit/src/constants/limits.ts` (`WISHLIST_DOC_ID` helper + `WISHLIST_COLLECTION`). |
| WL2 | Wishlist 20-item cap ÔÇö block on overflow + toast | M | Ôťů | S7 2026-05-11. `WishlistFullError { code, limit, current }` exported from appkit. `WISHLIST_MAX = 20` in `appkit/src/constants/limits.ts`. `addItem` is idempotent on existing productId and throws WishlistFullError at cap. API routes `/api/user/wishlist` + `/api/wishlist` + `/api/wishlist/merge` catch and return `409 { code, limit, current }` with toast-friendly message; GET responses now include `{ total, limit, isFull }`. `addToWishlistAction` returns a discriminated union `{ ok: true, count, limit, isFull } \| { ok: false, code: "WISHLIST_FULL", limit, current }`. Persistent banner + ÔÖí-button disabling on WishlistView/product cards deferred to WL3 (count badge). |
| WL3 | Wishlist count badge in user nav + page header | S | Ôťů S44 | `useWishlistCount()` hook (auth-only Ôćĺ `{count, limit, isFull}`) ÔÇö reads `wishlist-{userSlug}.items.length`. `count/20` chip in user dropdown nav and `/user/wishlist` header. Chip background amber at `>=18`, rose at `20`. SSR-hydrated. |
| WL4 | History one-doc-per-user schema (auth) ÔÇö 50 FIFO + re-visit hoist | M | Ôťů S44 | **New top-level collection** `history`. **One doc per user**: id === slug === `history-{userSlug}` (e.g. `history-user-mohsin-c`). Doc shape: `{ userId: "user-...", items: HistoryItem[], updatedAt }` where `HistoryItem = { productId, productType ("product"|"auction"|"preorder"), viewedAt, productSnapshot: { title, thumb, price, storeId, storeName } }`. Items ordered newest-first (position 0 = most recent). `historyRepository.track(userSlug, item)` in a **txn**: (a) read doc; (b) filter out any existing entry with same `productId` (re-visit removes old position); (c) unshift new entry at position 0; (d) if `items.length > 50` trim tail. Silent FIFO ÔÇö no error, no warning (auto-tracking, not user intent). `clearForUser(userSlug)` empties items. `removeOne(userSlug, productId)` splices by productId. Constant `HISTORY_MAX = 50` in `limits.ts`. Add `history-` to CLAUDE.md Slug Prefix table (id === slug). |
| WL5 | History guest mode ÔÇö localStorage with same cap + merge-on-login | S | Ôťů S44 | `useHistory()` hook: auth Ôćĺ POST `/api/user/history` (fire-and-forget, debounced); guest Ôćĺ `localStorage["letitrip:history"]` JSON array of HistoryItem (newest first, FIFO 50, same dedup-by-productId-and-unshift logic mirrored client-side). On login: `mergeGuestHistory()` reads localStorage Ôćĺ POSTs `/api/user/history/merge` with the array; server merges in a txn ÔÇö for each guest item, apply the same dedup+unshift+trim sequence (newest viewedAt wins on dedup). Clears localStorage on 2xx. |
| WL6 | History tracker integration + `/user/history` page | M | Ôťů S44 | Call `useHistory().track({productId, productType, snapshot})` on mount of `ProductDetailPageView`, `AuctionDetailPageView`, `PreOrderDetailPageView`. Debounce 1.5s (avoid bot/back-button spam). Session-scoped `Set<productId>` de-dups within a single page session. **New page** `/user/history`: SlottedListingView, no infinite scroll needed (single doc, ÔëĄ50 items), filter chips (All / Products / Auctions / Pre-orders), sort fixed `viewedAt desc`. Per-card "Remove" Ôćĺ `DELETE /api/user/history/[productId]`. Top "Clear all" Ôćĺ confirm modal Ôćĺ `DELETE /api/user/history`. Each card shows relative timestamp ("Visited 2 hours ago"). Empty state: "Nothing here yet ÔÇö products you view will appear here." Nav entry under User dashboard group. `ROUTES.USER.HISTORY`. |
| WL7 | Cart 50-distinct-items cap ÔÇö block on overflow + toast | S | Ôťů S44 | Server: `POST /api/cart/items` counts distinct items; if `>=50` **AND** new productId is not already in cart, return `409 { error:"CART_FULL", limit:50, current:50 }`. Per-item quantity increment is **unrestricted**. Constant `CART_MAX_ITEMS = 50` in `limits.ts`. Guest cart util (`appkit/src/features/cart/guestCart.ts`): same enforcement, same error code. Client toast variant=warning "Cart full (50/50). Remove items to add new ones." Persistent banner on `/cart` at cap. "Add to cart" buttons disabled + tooltip when cap reached. |
| WL8 | Seed + admin views + CLAUDE.md updates | M | Ôťů S44 | (1) `appkit/src/seed/history-seed-data.ts` ÔÇö 10 docs (one per buyer), each with 5ÔÇô30 HistoryItems across mixed productTypes, viewedAt spread over last 7 days, ordered newest-first. Wire into seed route (load/delete/count) + SeedPanel meta (slugPattern `history-{userSlug}`, no media, no PII). (2) Rebuild wishlist seed as 10 one-doc-per-user docs (`wishlist-{userSlug}`) with 1ÔÇô15 WishlistItems each. (3) `AdminWishlistsView` (LL15): switch to top-level `wishlistRepository.findAll()` returning user-level rows (user, item count, last updatedAt) ÔÇö drop `collectionGroup`; clicking a row opens a SideDrawer listing that user's items. (4) New `AdminHistoryView` read-only (similar pattern): rows = user + item count + last visit; row click Ôćĺ SideDrawer with HistoryItems. Nav: System group. API: `GET /api/admin/history`. (5) **No composite indexes needed** (single-doc reads) ÔÇö only the `firestore.rules` need allow-list updates for the two new collections. (6) Update CLAUDE.md: Collection Inventory rows for `wishlists` (new shape: one-doc-per-user, items[]) and `history` (new collection); add `wishlist-` and `history-` to Slug Prefix table (note: id === slug, like products/stores). |

| X8a | Extend Tailwind config + appkit tokens for layout utilities | M | Ôťů | Session 91 | Added --appkit-z-below/base/raised/tooltip to tokens.css; added component size tokens (input-sm/md/lg, avatar-xs/sm/md/lg); added grid-min-card tokens (xs/sm/default/lg). Rebuild appkit dist after. |

## Tier IX ÔÇö Component Quick-Reference Index *(in-editor greppable lookup)*

> `appkit/index.md` and `src/index.md` are the fast greppable indexes of all reusable components, utilities, and constants. **Authoritative deep docs live at `docs.letitrip.in` (Tier DX) ÔÇö these flat tables are the in-editor quick lookup only.**
> **Rule**: before creating any new component/util/constant, check the index. After every task that adds/renames/removes one, update the relevant row. Deep docs (stories, prop tables, usage examples) go in Tier DX, not here.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------|-------|
| IX1 | Create + maintain `appkit/index.md` + `src/index.md` component/util/constant indexes | S | Ôťů | 2026-05-08 | Initial index files created. Format: `\| Name \| Path \| What it does \|`. Covers: UI primitives (82 components), feature views (admin/seller/account/auth/etc.), hooks (85+), repositories (21), utils (18), constants. `src/index.md` covers app-level constants, server actions, routing components, and dev tools. **Update rule**: after every task that adds/removes/renames a component, util, or constant ÔÇö update the relevant row in the index. This prevents duplicate creation and speeds up future sessions. Deep docs (stories, prop tables, usage) go in Tier DX. |

---

## Tier DX ÔÇö Unified Docs Portal *(at docs.letitrip.in)*

> **Plan file**: `~/.claude/plans/say-what-is-better-glimmering-whale.md` ÔÇö full task specs, repo coverage matrix, site map, verification.
>
> **Why this tier exists**: consolidates developer docs (Storybook + Nextra + TypeDoc + OpenAPI) and end-user how-tos (Tier GD content) into one audience-scoped portal. Replaces Tier GD entirely; absorbs Tier IX's deeper-docs role (Tier IX `index.md` files remain as quick-reference). Spans **both** repos ÔÇö `appkit/` and `letitrip.in/src/`. Site map: `/developers` (engineers), `/help` (buyers), `/sellers` (store owners), `/employees` (admin + employee). Three in-app residuals (DX32ÔÇôDX34b) stay in the app because they depend on live user state.
>
> **Decisions**: subpackage `docs/` deployed at `docs.letitrip.in` (separate Vercel project, static-only ÔÇö Rule #6 safe). Full stack from day one. Admin/employee guides are publicly readable on docs (the real permission enforcement stays in the app ÔÇö these are docs, not data). No auth bridge. Tier IX `index.md` files kept as fast greppable lookup; new portal is authoritative.
>
> **Effort**: ~48 hrs across 7 phases; ship across 6ÔÇô8 sessions. Brand: `LetItRip` exactly (build-time grep gate fails on `Letitrip` / `LetiTrip` / `Let It Rip`).
>
> **Tracker conventions**: each DX row carries a one-line summary. Full specs (sections, fields, sub-sections, content sources) live in the plan file. The 22 Tier GD tasks below remain as content-source rows but are marked SUPERSEDED.

## Tier GP ÔÇö Grouped Listings *(standard products + pre-orders only; no auctions)*

> A "group" is a parent product linked to 1ÔÇôN child products (e.g., "Human Toy Complete Set" links to "head", "legs", "arms" as separate fully independent listings). Depth is exactly 1 ÔÇö no grandchildren. Each member has its own title, slug, price, images, and checkout flow. The group thread is visible as a collapsible "Show group (N items)" panel on every member's detail page.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------|-------|
| GP1 | Grouped listings schema + `ShowGroupSection` component | M | Ôťů | | **Schema** (`appkit/src/features/products/schemas/firestore.ts`): add to `ProductDocument`: `groupId?: string` (= parent slug; same on parent + all children), `isGroupParent?: boolean`, `groupParentSlug?: string` (null on parent; parent's slug on children), `groupChildSlugs?: string[]` (parent only), `groupTitle?: string` (e.g. "Human Toy Complete Set"). Slug convention: parent = `product-human-toy`; children append part name (`product-human-toy-head`). **New component** `appkit/src/features/products/components/ShowGroupSection.tsx` ÔÇö receives `groupId` + `currentSlug` + `isParent` props; renders nothing if `groupId` absent. Fetches all products/pre-orders with matching `groupId`. **Parent view**: collapsible panel "Parts in this group (N)". **Child view**: collapsible panel "Part of: [groupTitle]". Both collapsed by default. **Card style**: small circular thumbnail cards (~64 px) in a `HorizontalScroller`; cards are selectable ÔÇö clicking navigates to that member's detail page; current product has a highlighted ring border. Parent card shown first with a "Set" badge. **"View whole group Ôćĺ" button** opens a `Modal` (or `SideDrawer` if Ôëą 5 parts) with a table ÔÇö columns: thumbnail (click to expand image preview), name, price, condition, "View" link. Standard products + pre-orders only. **Placement**: injected via a new `renderGroupSection` render prop on `ProductDetailView` and the pre-order equivalent ÔÇö rendered between the buy-box/actions area and the TABS row (NOT in `belowFold`). `npx tsc --noEmit` Ôćĺ 0 errors. |
| GP2 | Edit-screen "Group settings" panel + inline child creation + link-existing | M | Ôťů | | Depends on GP1. Add collapsible **"Group settings"** section to `AdminProductEditorView` and seller `ProductForm.tsx`. Hidden on auction forms. **Three states**: *(1) Not in a group* ÔÇö "Start a group" button Ôćĺ sets `isGroupParent: true`, `groupId: this.slug`. *(2) This is the group parent* ÔÇö shows `groupTitle` input; lists children (thumbnail, title, price, condition, "Unlink" button in batch write); **"Add child listing"** button Ôćĺ modal with **two tabs**: **Tab 1 ÔÇö Create new child**: minimal form with only the fields that differ (title, slug auto-suggested as `parent-slug-[part]`, price, short description, condition, images via MediaUploadField); all other fields (category, brand, storeId, tags, shippingInfo, returnPolicy) shown as read-only "Inherited from parent" badges; on save: creates new product doc with inherited fields + minimal changes; updates parent `groupChildSlugs` atomically; toast; "Need more control? Edit the full listing after saving" note. **Tab 2 ÔÇö Link existing**: searchable `DynamicSelect` across products + pre-orders by title or slug; validates: candidate not already in a group, not an auction; on confirm: batch-writes `groupId`/`groupParentSlug` onto the linked listing + adds its slug to parent `groupChildSlugs`. Also: "Dissolve group" button (confirm required) Ôćĺ batch-clears all group fields on parent + all children. *(3) This is a child* ÔÇö "Part of: [groupTitle]" read-only banner with link to parent edit page; "Leave group" button (confirm). All multi-doc writes are atomic batch. |

## Tier SC ÔÇö Sub-listing Categories *(all listing types: products, auctions, pre-orders)*

> A "sub-listing category" is a named bucket (e.g., "Base Set 1 Charizard 108/120") that groups multiple independent listings of the same real-world collectible with different conditions, grades, prices, and sellers. Each listing is still its own full product/auction/pre-order ÔÇö the sub-listing category is just the thread linking them. The public page shows all members. The detail page shows a collapsible horizontal scroller "More listings in: [name]".

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------|-------|
| SC1 | Sub-listing categories ÔÇö schema + repository + API routes | M | Ôťů | | **New Firestore collection**: `sublisting_categories`. **`SublistingCategoryDocument`** type (new file `appkit/src/features/products/schemas/sublisting-categories.ts` or add to categories schema): `id: string` (= slug), `slug: string` (prefix: `sublisting-`), `name: string`, `itemCode?: string` (e.g. "108/120", "PSA-10"), `description?: string`, `coverImage?: string` (`/media/<slug>` proxy URL), `productCount: number` (maintained via batch write), `createdAt: Date`, `updatedAt: Date`, `createdBy: string`. **New field on `ProductDocument`** (and auction/pre-order if separate schemas): `sublistingCategoryId?: string` (a listing belongs to at most 1 sub-listing category). **`SublistingCategoriesRepository`** ÔÇö same pattern as `CategoriesRepository`: `findById`, `findBySlug`, `list(model)` (Sieve pagination), `create`, `update`, `delete`, `getListingsByCategoryId(id, limit?)` (returns products + auctions + pre-orders with matching `sublistingCategoryId`, ordered by price, default limit 10). **API routes**: `GET /api/admin/sublisting-categories` (list + search), `POST /api/admin/sublisting-categories` (create), `GET /api/admin/sublisting-categories/[id]` (get one), `PUT /api/admin/sublisting-categories/[id]` (update), `DELETE /api/admin/sublisting-categories/[id]` (delete ÔÇö unlinks all members first by batch-clearing their `sublistingCategoryId`), `GET /api/sublisting-categories/[slug]` (public ÔÇö returns category + first 20 listings), `GET /api/sublisting-categories/[slug]/listings` (paginated public listings). | SC3 | `sublistingCategoryId` field on all listing forms + `SublistingCarouselSection` component | M | Ôťů | | Depends on SC1. **Form field** (this is the ONLY way listings are linked to sub-listing categories ÔÇö no central "assign products" UI): add "Sub-listing category" `DynamicSelect` to product/pre-order/auction create+edit forms, pulling from `/api/admin/sublisting-categories`. Zero fuzzy search, zero third-party dependency ÔÇö all suggestions come from existing Firestore data.

## Tier ARCH ÔÇö Store Identity Architecture *(storeId/storeName public; sellerId = internal auth only)*

> **Core rule**: The store is the public identity on LetiTrip ÔÇö not the individual seller user behind it. Public-facing APIs, UI cards, detail pages, cart items, and profiles must show `storeId` / `storeName` / `storeSlug`. The Firebase UID of the store owner (`sellerId` internally) is an auth/internal field only ÔÇö it must never appear in a public API response or client-rendered prop. Admin views may additionally display `ownerId` (display alias for `sellerId` in admin context). Server-only code (checkout, analytics, payout calculation, authorization) may continue using `sellerId` for auth logic without change.
>
> **SideDrawer vs Modal rule** (enforced from this tier forward): 0 fields Ôćĺ `ConfirmDeleteModal`; 1ÔÇô2 fields Ôćĺ `Modal`; 3+ fields Ôćĺ `SideDrawer`.
>
> **User roles** (public 3-tier): `user` (basic buyer) | `seller` (has Ôëą1 store) | `admin` (platform admin). `moderator` is an internal sub-role of admin.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------|-------|
| ARCH1 | Public API sanitization: strip sellerId from product/review/order public responses | M | Ôťů | S6 2026-05-11 | New `sanitizeProductForPublic`/`sanitizeProductsForPublic` helper in `appkit/src/features/products/utils/sanitize.ts` (strips sellerId/sellerName/sellerEmail/ownerId). Wired into appkit `products/api/route.ts` GET list, appkit `products/api/[id]/route.ts` GET detail, and letitrip `src/app/api/products/route.ts` GET. Reviews + orders already had no sellerId in public responses ÔÇö no change. |
| ARCH2 | Cart items: sellerId/sellerName Ôćĺ storeId/storeName | M | Ôťů | Session 81 | Cart/Order/Coupon/Offer/Payout schemas all migrated. Checkout two-step shipping lookup (storeIdÔćĺownerIdÔćĺuser). Bid guard fixed. All seed data updated. All repositories renamed (findBySellerÔćĺfindByStore etc.). ProductItem type gained storeName. Both appkit and main app pass tsc --noEmit 0 errors. |

## Tier SEO ÔÇö Lighthouse & Search Engine Optimisation *(post-alpha, before RBAC)*

> **Goal**: Achieve Lighthouse Performance Ôëą 90 and eliminate crawlability gaps on all public pages. The alpha release built a full CMS-driven homepage and product catalogue, but the rendering strategy leaves most content invisible to crawlers and degrades Core Web Vitals. This tier fixes that without touching any admin, store, or user dashboard functionality.
>
> **Root problems identified (2026-05-10 audit)**:
> 1. Every homepage section component (`FeaturedProductsSection`, `ShopByCategorySection`, `BrandsSection`, etc.) is `"use client"` and fetches its own data via hooks ÔÇö Googlebot sees empty skeletons in initial HTML; product/auction/brand/category content is absent from the page source.
> 2. `HeroCarousel` receives `initialSlides` as a prop from the server but renders everything client-side ÔÇö the first-slide image (the LCP element) cannot be `priority`-loaded; crawlers get no slide content.
> 3. `ProductGrid.tsx` (lines ~100 and ~413) uses `style={{ backgroundImage: url(...) }}` ÔÇö images are not optimised by Next.js (no WebP/AVIF, no `srcset`, no lazy-load control, no LCP eligibility).
> 4. JSON-LD helpers (`productJsonLd`, `auctionJsonLd`, `blogPostJsonLd`, etc.) exist in `appkit/src/seo/json-ld.ts` but are called nowhere ÔÇö no rich snippets (price, ratings, breadcrumbs, article byline) appear in Google search results.
> 5. 15+ public pages (`/sellers`, `/help`, `/contact`, `/how-*/`, `/fees`, `/security`, etc.) export no `metadata` at all ÔÇö no title, description, or Open Graph tags.
> 6. Paginated and filtered routes (`/search/[...]/page/[n]`, `/categories/[slug]/tab/.../page/[page]`) have no canonical URL ÔÇö Google may penalise for duplicate content.
>
> **Constraints**: All fixes are in `appkit/src/` or `src/` only. No admin, store, or user dashboard pages are touched. No Firestore schemas change. The carousel and homepage section CMS (CF1, HS1ÔÇôHS5) remain exactly as-is ÔÇö only the public render path changes. VD3 is subsumed into SEO5.
>
> **Do SEO1 Ôćĺ SEO2 Ôćĺ SEO3 Ôćĺ SEO4 Ôćĺ SEO5 Ôćĺ SEO6 Ôćĺ SEO7 in order** (each is independently deployable but they compound ÔÇö do not skip).

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| SEO1 | Homepage sections: SSR data hydration so carousel content appears in initial HTML | L | Ôťů | Session 82 | **Problem**: `FeaturedProductsSection`, `FeaturedAuctionsSection`, `FeaturedPreOrdersSection`, `FeaturedStoresSection`, `ShopByCategorySection`, `BrandsSection`, `BlogArticlesSection`, `EventsSection` all fetch their own data client-side via hooks (`useFeaturedProducts`, `useFeaturedAuctions`, etc.). | SEO2 | HeroCarousel: render first slide in SSR HTML + `priority` image for LCP | M | Ôťů | Session 82 ÔÇö `initialSlides` already threaded from server; first slide background uses `priority={slideIndex===0}`. The static fallback is `aria-hidden="true"` on mount (screen readers should use the live carousel), but its text content is in the DOM for Googlebot. First slide `MediaImage` always gets `priority={true}` and `sizes="100vw"`. Subsequent slides remain lazy. **Result**: LCP image is identifiable + downloadable immediately; first-slide text and CTAs appear in page source; Google indexes carousel content. `npx tsc --noEmit` Ôćĺ 0 errors. |

Add a `minHeight?: number | string` prop to `HorizontalScroller` and `SectionCarousel`. Pass card-appropriate values: product/auction cards `320px`, store cards `200px`, brand logos `80px`, category tiles `160px`. The scroller container applies `style={{ minHeight }}` before JS runs, reserving space and eliminating the CLS jump. `npx tsc --noEmit` Ôćĺ 0 errors. |

---

## Tier RBAC ÔÇö Permission-Based Access Control *(low priority)*

> **­čôÉ Layered shape (S14+):** auth is cross-cutting ÔÇö server code lives at `appkit/src/_internal/server/auth/` (new sub-tree), not as a `features/<x>/` entry.
> - **Constants:** `_internal/shared/features/auth/config.ts` ÔÇö `PERMISSIONS`, `PERMISSION_GROUPS`.
> - **Types:** `_internal/shared/features/auth/types.ts` ÔÇö `Permission`, `PermissionGroup`, `RoleResolution`.
> - **Validation:** `_internal/shared/features/auth/schema.ts` ÔÇö Zod for permission patches.
> - **Data layer:** `_internal/server/auth/permissions/{resolver,data}.ts` ÔÇö `resolvePermissions(uid)`, `getEmployee(uid)`.
> - **Business logic:** `_internal/server/auth/middleware.ts` ÔÇö `assertPermission()`, `assertRole()`; errors `ForbiddenError`, `RoleMismatchError`.
> - **Actions:** `_internal/server/features/team/actions.ts` ÔÇö `inviteEmployee`, `updateEmployeePermissions`, `revokeEmployee` (`"use server"`).
> - **Repository:** extend `usersRepository` for `permissions[]` + `permissionGroup`.
> - **Orchestration:** Cloud Function on user role change Ôćĺ `setCustomUserClaims(uid, { admin: true })` (jobs handler `_internal/server/jobs/handlers/onUserRoleChange.ts`).
> - **Views:** `TeamManagementView`, `EmployeeEditorView`, gated `AdminLayoutShell` variants.
> - **Consumer wiring:** `[locale]/admin/layout.tsx` SSR gate; per-section `[locale]/admin/<x>/layout.tsx`; `[locale]/admin/team/page.tsx`; `src/proxy.ts` first-gate.
> - **OG + sitemap:** **N/A** (admin-only).
> - **Error handling:** anonymous Ôćĺ `notFound()`; logged-in but missing perm Ôćĺ `/unauthorized` page (403); team API Ôćĺ typed JSON `{ error, code }`.
> - **Verification:** anonymous Ôćĺ 404 on every gated route; permission-table snapshot test; Firestore rules dry-run via emulator; `tsc` 0/0; `audit-violations` exit 0.

> **Design intent**: Implement a granular, permission-based access control system layered on top of the existing role system. This enables hiring interns/employees (e.g. content moderator, finance manager, ad manager, SEO manager, blog poster, event handler, review manager, site manager) who each get a tailored subset of admin panel access ÔÇö without ever granting them the full `admin` role. All permission checks are SSR-enforced (Server Components + API route guards) so users cannot manipulate their own access via browser devtools.
>
> **Core model**: `admin` role = full access (bypasses all checks). New `employee` role = access determined entirely by `permissions: Permission[]` field on their `UserDocument`. Roles are bundles of permissions at setup time; each individual employee can have custom overrides on top of their preset group.
>
> **Permission naming convention**: `admin:resource:action` (e.g. `admin:blog:publish`, `admin:payouts:write`, `admin:events:delete`).
>
> **Enforcement layers (in order)**:
> 1. `proxy.ts` middleware ÔÇö role gate: is user `admin` or `employee`? If neither, redirect to `/unauthorized` before any page renders.
> 2. `src/app/[locale]/admin/layout.tsx` (RSC) ÔÇö fetches `permissions[]` from Firestore server-side; checks `admin:dashboard:view`; redirects if absent.
> 3. Section-level `layout.tsx` files (RSC) ÔÇö each admin route group gets its own layout that checks the section-specific permission (e.g. `/admin/blog/layout.tsx` checks `admin:blog:read`).
> 4. API routes ÔÇö `requirePermission(request, permission)` wrapper applied to every admin API endpoint; admin role bypasses.
> 5. Firestore security rules ÔÇö users cannot write their own `permissions`, `role`, or `permissionGroup` fields; only Admin SDK (server) can.
>
> **Employee preset groups (16 bundles ÔÇö assigned at invite time, customisable per-user)**:
>
> | Group | Typical intern role | Permissions granted |
> |---|---|---|
> | `content_moderator` | Content intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:reviews:read/write/delete`, `admin:products:read`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:blog:read` |
> | `review_manager` | Review intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:reviews:read/write/delete`, `admin:products:read`, `admin:users:read` |
> | `blog_poster` | Blog writer | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:blog:read/write` (NOT delete, NOT publish), `admin:media:read/write` |
> | `community_manager` | Social/community | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:events:read/write/delete`, `admin:event-entries:read/write`, `admin:blog:read/write/publish`, `admin:reviews:read`, `admin:notifications:read/write`, `admin:newsletter:read/write`, `admin:media:read/write` |
> | `event_handler` | Events intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:events:read/write/delete`, `admin:event-entries:read/write`, `admin:notifications:read/write` |
> | `newsletter_manager` | Email marketing | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:newsletter:read/write`, `admin:contact:read`, `admin:users:read` |
> | `seo_manager` | SEO intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:faqs:read/write/delete`, `admin:blog:read/write/publish`, `admin:navigation:read/write`, `admin:sections:read/write`, `admin:site:read` |
> | `ad_manager` | Ads intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:ads:read/write/delete`, `admin:carousel:read/write/delete`, `admin:deals:read/write`, `admin:featured:read/write`, `admin:sections:read/write` |
> | `site_manager` | Site/CMS manager | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:site:read/write`, `admin:navigation:read/write`, `admin:sections:read/write`, `admin:carousel:read/write`, `admin:faqs:read/write`, `admin:media:read/write` |
> | `catalog_manager` | Catalog intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:categories:read/write/delete`, `admin:brands:read/write/delete`, `admin:products:read/write`, `admin:media:read/write`, `admin:deals:read/write`, `admin:featured:read/write` |
> | `finance_manager` | Finance intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:analytics:view`, `admin:payouts:read/write`, `admin:orders:read`, `admin:returns:read` |
> | `data_analyst` | Analytics (read-only) | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:analytics:view`, `admin:orders:read`, `admin:payouts:read`, `admin:products:read`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:reviews:read`, `admin:carts:read`, `admin:wishlists:read`, `admin:bids:read` |
> | `customer_support` | Support agent | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:orders:read/write`, `admin:returns:read/write`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:contact:read`, `admin:notifications:read/write` |
> | `store_onboarding` | Seller success | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:stores:read/write`, `admin:store-addresses:read`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:notifications:write` |
> | `trust_and_safety` | Trust & safety | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:users:read/write`, `admin:orders:read`, `admin:products:read/write`, `admin:reviews:read/write/delete`, `admin:bids:read/write`, `admin:sessions:read/delete`, `admin:carts:read` |
> | `auction_monitor` | Auction intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:bids:read/write`, `admin:products:read`, `admin:orders:read`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:notifications:write` |
> | `scam_moderator` | Scam/trust intern | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:scammers:read/write/verify/delete`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:media:read/write` |
> | `support_agent` | Customer support | `admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:support-tickets:read/write/assign/close`, `admin:orders:read/write`, `admin:returns:read/write`, `admin:users:read`, `admin:contact:read`, `admin:notifications:read/write` |
>
> **Store capabilities (per-store flags)**: stored as `capabilities?: StoreCapability[]` on `StoreDocument`. Managed by admin via `AdminStoreEditorView`. Checked server-side on every relevant store API route ÔÇö client visibility is UX only, not security. Available capabilities split into two tiers:
>
> **Listing & Catalog capabilities** (control what types of listings a store can create):
>
> | Capability | Default | What it unlocks |
> |---|---|---|
> | `host_auctions` | ÔťŚ | Can create auction listings (`/store/auctions`). Not all stores are trusted to run auctions ÔÇö requires admin approval. |
> | `host_preorders` | ÔťŚ | Can create pre-order listings (`/store/pre-orders`). Indicates store has a supplier relationship. |
> | `create_categories` | ÔťŚ | Can request new category creation from the storefront (goes to admin for approval). Power sellers only. |
> | `suggest_brands` | Ôťô | Can suggest new brands via form (admin reviews before publishing). On by default for all stores. |
> | `create_coupons` | Ôťô | Can create store-level coupons (`/store/coupons`). On by default. |
> | `bulk_listing_import` | ÔťŚ | Can bulk-import products via CSV template. Requires admin setup of import schema per store. |
> | `extended_return_window` | ÔťŚ | Store can offer 30-day returns (platform default is 7 days). Contractual agreement required. |
>
> **Trust & Visibility capabilities** (control how a store appears on the platform):
>
> | Capability | Default | What it unlocks |
> |---|---|---|
> | `verified_seller` | ÔťŚ | Shows "Verified" badge on store profile + product cards. Admin manually grants after identity verification. |
> | `featured_placement` | ÔťŚ | Store is eligible to appear in featured stores sections and homepage store rows. |
> | `promotional_banner` | ÔťŚ | Store's banner can be used in homepage carousel / promotional sections by admin. |
> | `priority_support` | ÔťŚ | Store queries go to a dedicated support queue with faster SLA. |
>
> **Platform & Technical capabilities** (control platform-level privileges):
>
> | Capability | Default | What it unlocks |
> |---|---|---|
> | `multiple_stores` | ÔťŚ | Owner can create more than one store (default: 1 per user). Admin grants per seller agreement. |
> | `custom_store_slug` | ÔťŚ | Can change their store URL slug after initial setup (default: locked after first 7 days). |
> | `api_access` | ÔťŚ | Store gets API credentials for programmatic product/order access (future: for power sellers with integrations). |
> | `lower_commission_rate` | ÔťŚ | Negotiated reduced platform commission. Requires a `customCommissionRate: number` field on `StoreDocument` alongside this capability. |
> | `early_access_features` | ÔťŚ | Store sees beta features before GA (e.g. new listing types, new analytics views). |
> | `advanced_analytics` | ÔťŚ | Access to detailed analytics (cohort retention, basket analysis, top-buyer breakdown). Standard stores get summary only. |
>
> **Do RBAC1 Ôćĺ RBAC3 Ôćĺ RBAC10 Ôćĺ RBAC5 Ôćĺ RBAC4 Ôćĺ RBAC7 Ôćĺ RBAC6 Ôćĺ RBAC8 Ôćĺ RBAC9 in order** (each task depends on the previous).

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| RBAC1 | Permission constants + UserDocument schema extension | S | Ôťů | **New file** `appkit/src/features/auth/permissions/constants.ts`: (1) `Permission` union type ÔÇö all ~85 permission strings: core admin (`admin:dashboard:view`, `admin:users:read/write/delete`, `admin:products:read/write/delete`, `admin:orders:read/write`, `admin:returns:read/write`, `admin:stores:read/write`, `admin:store-addresses:read`, `admin:analytics:view`, `admin:payouts:read/write`, `admin:categories:read/write/delete`, `admin:brands:read/write/delete`, `admin:coupons:read/write/delete`, `admin:deals:read/write`, `admin:featured:read/write`, `admin:reviews:read/write/delete`, `admin:blog:read/write/delete/publish`, `admin:bids:read/write`, `admin:media:read/write/delete`, `admin:site:read/write`, `admin:navigation:read/write`, `admin:sections:read/write`, `admin:carousel:read/write/delete`, `admin:ads:read/write/delete`, `admin:faqs:read/write/delete`, `admin:newsletter:read/write`, `admin:contact:read`, `admin:events:read/write/delete`, `admin:event-entries:read/write`, `admin:sessions:read/delete`, `admin:notifications:read/write`, `admin:carts:read`, `admin:wishlists:read`, `admin:feature-flags:read/write`, `admin:copilot:view`, `admin:team:read/write`); **moderation** (`admin:user-bans:read`, `admin:user-bans:write`, `admin:support-tickets:read`, `admin:support-tickets:write`, `admin:support-tickets:assign`, `admin:support-tickets:close`); **scam** (`admin:scammers:read`, `admin:scammers:write`, `admin:scammers:verify`, `admin:scammers:delete`). (2) `EmployeeGroup` union (18 presets + custom): `"content_moderator" \| "review_manager" \| "blog_poster" \| "community_manager" \| "event_handler" \| "newsletter_manager" \| "seo_manager" \| "ad_manager" \| "site_manager" \| "catalog_manager" \| "finance_manager" \| "data_analyst" \| "customer_support" \| "store_onboarding" \| "trust_and_safety" \| "auction_monitor" \| "scam_moderator" \| "support_agent" \| "custom"`. (3) `PERMISSION_GROUPS: Record<EmployeeGroup, Permission[]>` ÔÇö all 18 preset bundles per the table above. (4) `ROUTE_PERMISSION_MAP: Record<string, Permission>` ÔÇö maps each `/admin/[section]` path to its required read permission. (5) `StoreCapability` union (18 capabilities across 3 tiers). **Schema extension** in `appkit/src/features/auth/schemas/firestore.ts`: add `"employee"` to `UserRole` union; add `permissions?: Permission[]` and `permissionGroup?: EmployeeGroup` to `UserDocument`; add `capabilities?: StoreCapability[]` and `customCommissionRate?: number` to `StoreDocument`. Export all new types from `appkit/src/features/auth/client.ts` and `server.ts`. `npx tsc --noEmit` Ôćĺ 0 errors in both repos. |
| RBAC2 | Server-side permission resolver | M | Ôťů | Depends on RBAC1. **New file** `appkit/src/features/auth/server/getServerPermissions.ts`: (1) `getServerPermissions(uid: string): Promise<Permission[]>` ÔÇö fetches user doc from Firestore Admin SDK; if `role === "admin"` returns a sentinel `ALL_PERMISSIONS` constant (all permissions granted); if `role === "employee"` returns `user.permissions ?? []`; for any other role returns `[]`. (2) `hasPermission(permissions: Permission[], required: Permission): boolean` ÔÇö pure check; if `permissions === ALL_PERMISSIONS` always returns true. (3) `hasAnyPermission(permissions: Permission[], required: Permission[]): boolean`. (4) `requirePermission(request: NextRequest, permission: Permission): Promise<UserDocument>` ÔÇö wraps `requireAuthFromRequest` + `getServerPermissions`; throws `NextResponse.json({ error: "Forbidden" }, { status: 403 })` if permission absent; admin bypasses. Export from `appkit` server barrel. |
| RBAC3 | Admin layout SSR permission gate | M | Ôťů | Depends on RBAC2. Convert `src/app/[locale]/admin/layout.tsx` from client `<ProtectedRoute requireRole="admin">` to a **Server Component**: (1) call `getServerSessionUser()` ÔÇö if null, `redirect(ROUTES.AUTH.LOGIN)`; (2) if `user.role !== "admin" && user.role !== "employee"`, `redirect("/unauthorized")`; (3) call `getServerPermissions(user.uid)` ÔÇö if does not include `admin:dashboard:view`, `redirect("/unauthorized")`; (4) pass `{ user, permissions }` as props to a new `AdminLayoutShell` client component (the existing sidebar/layout UI stays client-side). The shell component shows only nav items the employee has permission to see (RBAC7 wires this). Keep existing visual layout identical ÔÇö only auth logic changes. Ensure the shell receives `permissions` as a serialisable prop (string array). `npx tsc --noEmit` Ôćĺ 0 errors. |

| RBAC5 | API route permission guards | M | Ôťů | Depends on RBAC2. Apply `requirePermission(request, permission)` to every admin API route that currently uses `requireRoleFromRequest(request, ["admin"])`. Example: `src/app/api/admin/blog/route.ts` GET Ôćĺ `admin:blog:read`; POST Ôćĺ `admin:blog:write`; `admin/blog/[id]/route.ts` DELETE Ôćĺ `admin:blog:delete`.
