| RBAC9 | Firestore security rules ÔÇö block permission self-escalation | S | Ôťů | Depends on RBAC1. Update `appkit/firebase/base/firestore.rules` (the base file that feeds into the root `firestore.rules` via `firebase-merge.mjs`). Add rules to the `/users/{userId}` match block: (1) Disallow any authenticated user from writing `role`, `permissions`, or `permissionGroup` fields on their own document ÔÇö these fields can only be written by the Admin SDK (which bypasses Firestore rules entirely via service account). Implementation: `allow write: if false` on a rule that triggers when `request.resource.data.diff(resource.data).affectedKeys().hasAny(["role", "permissions", "permissionGroup"])` ÔÇö unless the requesting user is a verified admin (check `request.auth.token.admin == true` from custom claims). (2) Add custom claim `admin: true` to the Admin SDK token via `setCustomUserClaims(uid, { admin: true })` in a Cloud Function triggered on user role change ÔÇö this ensures Firestore rules can distinguish Admin SDK writes from client writes. After: run `firebase emulators:start` and verify a client write to `permissions` field is rejected with `PERMISSION_DENIED`. Run `firebase-merge.mjs` before deploying. |
| RBAC10 | Proxy.ts middleware first gate | S | Ôťů | Depends on RBAC1. Extend `src/proxy.ts` (Next.js 16 middleware file) to add a cheap first gate for `/admin/*` routes: (1) Extract session cookie (`__session`) ÔÇö verify via Firebase Admin SDK `verifySessionCookie()` (already available in middleware context). (2) Read `role` from the decoded token or from a minimal Firestore read (use a cached read ÔÇö `getServerSessionUser()` equivalent). (3) If role is not `"admin"` and not `"employee"`: immediately return `NextResponse.redirect(new URL("/unauthorized", request.url))` ÔÇö do NOT let the page render at all. (4) If role is `"admin"`: allow through without any further check (full access). (5) If role is `"employee"`: allow through ÔÇö the RSC layout (RBAC3) will do the fine-grained permission check with a Firestore read. **Important**: do NOT do a full Firestore permission read in middleware ÔÇö it runs on Edge and Firestore Admin SDK may not be available there. Keep the middleware check role-only; the full permission enforcement happens in the Server Component layouts. Also add `/unauthorized` to the public route allowlist (never redirect the unauthorized page itself). |

---

## Tier BAN ÔÇö User Moderation & Trust *(low priority)*

> **­čôÉ Layered shape (S14+):**
> - **Constants:** `_internal/shared/features/moderation/config.ts` ÔÇö `BAN_TYPES`, `BAN_REASONS`, `SUPPORT_TICKET_LIMITS`, `BANNED_ACTIONS`.
> - **Types:** `_internal/shared/features/moderation/types.ts` ÔÇö `BanDocument`, `UserSoftBan`, `BannedAction`, `SupportTicketDocument`, `SupportTicketStatus`.
> - **Validation:** `_internal/shared/features/moderation/schema.ts` ÔÇö Zod for ban patches + ticket creation/response.
> - **Data layer:** `_internal/server/features/moderation/data.ts` ÔÇö `getBanFor(uid)`, `listTickets(uid)`, `getTicketSummary()`.
> - **Business logic:** `_internal/server/features/moderation/service.ts` ÔÇö `assertNotHardBanned(uid)`, `assertNotSoftBannedFor(uid, action)`, `assertSupportTicketLimit(uid)`; errors `HardBanError`, `SoftBanError`, `SupportTicketLimitError`.
> - **Actions:** `_internal/server/features/moderation/actions.ts` ÔÇö `createBan`, `liftBan`, `cascadeHardBan`, `createTicket`, `respondToTicket` (`"use server"`).
> - **Repository:** new `bansRepository`, `supportTicketsRepository` in `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/moderation/repository.ts`.
> - **Orchestration:** `_internal/server/jobs/handlers/{banLifecycle,supportTicketSla,banExpiryCleanup}.ts`.
> - **Views:** `AdminBansView`, `AdminTicketsView`, `UserSupportPageView`, `UserBanNoticePageView`, guest-checkout block component.
> - **Consumer wiring:** `[locale]/admin/bans/page.tsx`, `[locale]/admin/tickets/page.tsx`, `[locale]/user/support/page.tsx`, `[locale]/banned/page.tsx`; checkout page guest-block.
> - **OG + sitemap:** **N/A**.
> - **Error handling:** hard-ban Ôćĺ session cleared + redirect to `/banned`; soft-ban Ôćĺ mutate API rejects with inline form error; ticket-over-limit Ôćĺ toast "You have 2 active tickets ÔÇö close one first".
> - **Verification:** soft-banned user can read but every gated mutate returns 403; hard-ban cascade clears all sessions + cancels active bids + suspends listings; ticket lifecycle Function dry-run; `tsc` 0/0.

> **Design intent**: Give LetItRip admins fine-grained control over user behaviour without needing the nuclear option of a full account ban for every infraction. A soft ban restricts specific actions (writing reviews, joining events, placing bids, etc.) while letting the user continue browsing. A hard ban disables the Firebase Auth account entirely and cascades to suspend listings, cancel active bids, and revoke sessions. The support ticket system is built here because it is the primary channel through which bans get contested and resolved.
>
> **Soft ban model**: `UserDocument.softBans: UserSoftBan[]` ÔÇö an array of scoped restrictions. Each entry has `action: BannedAction`, `reason: string`, `bannedBy: string` (employee uid), `bannedAt: Date`, `expiresAt?: Date` (null = permanent). Supported `BannedAction` values: `write_reviews`, `write_blog_comments`, `join_events`, `place_bids`, `create_listings`, `send_messages`, `create_support_tickets`, `report_scammers`. A user may have multiple simultaneous soft bans of different types.
>
> **Hard ban model**: `isDisabled: true` (already on `UserDocument`) + `hardBanReason?: string` + `hardBannedAt?: Date` + `hardBannedBy?: string`. Triggers Firebase Auth `updateUser(uid, { disabled: true })` via Admin SDK.
>
> **Support ticket rules** (enforced server-side, no client trust):
> - Max **2 active** (status: `open` | `in_progress` | `waiting_on_user`) general tickets per user at any time.
> - Order tickets: exactly **1 per non-completed order** (orders in status `PENDING`, `PROCESSING`, `SHIPPED`, `RETURN_REQUESTED` only ÔÇö not `DELIVERED`, `CANCELLED`, `REFUNDED`).
> - Guests cannot create tickets ÔÇö authentication required.
> - If user has `create_support_tickets` soft ban Ôćĺ 403 "Your account is restricted from opening support tickets."
> - New ticket in same category not allowed while an existing one in that category is in `waiting_on_user` status (prevents spam reopening).
>
> **Notification routing (Firebase Functions)**: ticket events Ôćĺ notify user + notify all employees who have `admin:support-tickets:read` permission. Ban events Ôćĺ notify user + notify all employees with `admin:user-bans:read` permission. Notifications written to the `notifications` Firestore collection (existing schema) + Firebase Cloud Messaging push if device token present.
>
> **Do BAN1 Ôćĺ BAN2 Ôćĺ BAN3 Ôćĺ BAN4 Ôćĺ BAN5 Ôćĺ BAN6 Ôćĺ BAN7 Ôćĺ BAN8 Ôćĺ BAN9 in order.**

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| BAN1 | Schema ÔÇö ban fields on UserDocument + SupportTicket collection | S | Ôťů | **(1) UserDocument additions** in `appkit/src/features/auth/schemas/firestore.ts`: `softBans?: UserSoftBan[]`; `hardBanReason?: string`; `hardBannedAt?: Timestamp`; `hardBannedBy?: string`. **New types** `BannedAction = "write_reviews" \| "write_blog_comments" \| "join_events" \| "place_bids" \| "create_listings" \| "send_messages" \| "create_support_tickets" \| "report_scammers"` and `UserSoftBan = { action: BannedAction; reason: string; bannedBy: string; bannedAt: Timestamp; expiresAt?: Timestamp \| null }`. **(2) New collection** `supportTickets` ÔÇö new file `appkit/src/features/support/schemas/firestore.ts`. `SupportTicketDocument`: `id` (prefix `ticket-`, auto-ID), `userId: string`, `userEmail: string` (denormalized), `userDisplayName: string`, `category: TicketCategory`, `subject: string`, `description: string`, `orderId?: string` (linked when category=`order_issue`), `status: TicketStatus`, `priority: "low" \| "normal" \| "high" \| "urgent"`, `assignedTo?: string` (employee uid), `assignedToName?: string`, `internalNotes?: string` (admin-only, never sent to user), `messages: TicketMessage[]`, `resolvedAt?: Timestamp`, `closedAt?: Timestamp`, `createdAt: Timestamp`, `updatedAt: Timestamp`. **`TicketCategory`**: `"order_issue" \| "billing_payment" \| "account" \| "listing_dispute" \| "scam_report" \| "refund_request" \| "auction_dispute" \| "general"`. **`TicketStatus`**: `"open" \| "in_progress" \| "waiting_on_user" \| "resolved" \| "closed"`. **`TicketMessage`**: `{ id: string; authorId: string; authorRole: "user" \| "support" \| "admin"; body: string; attachments?: string[]; createdAt: Timestamp }`. Add `SupportRepository` stub (`appkit/src/repositories/support.repository.ts`) with methods: `createTicket`, `getUserTickets(userId)`, `getTicketById`, `countActiveTickets(userId)`, `getActiveOrderTicket(userId, orderId)`, `updateTicketStatus`, `addMessage`, `assignTicket`. Export from appkit. `npx tsc --noEmit` Ôćĺ 0 errors. |
| BAN2 | Soft ban enforcement ÔÇö server-side action guards | M | Ôťů | Depends on BAN1. Create `appkit/src/features/auth/server/checkSoftBan.ts`: `isSoftBanned(user: UserDocument, action: BannedAction): boolean` ÔÇö checks `user.softBans[]`; ignores entries where `expiresAt` is in the past (expired bans are treated as lifted without deletion). **Wire enforcement into API routes**: (1) `POST /api/reviews` Ôćĺ check `write_reviews`; (2) `POST /api/blog/[id]/comments` (future) Ôćĺ check `write_blog_comments`; (3) `POST /api/events/[id]/entries` Ôćĺ check `join_events`; (4) `POST /api/bids` Ôćĺ check `place_bids`; (5) `POST /api/store/products` (and auction/preorder) Ôćĺ check `create_listings` (on the seller's user doc); (6) `POST /api/support/tickets` Ôćĺ check `create_support_tickets`; (7) `POST /api/scammers/report` Ôćĺ check `report_scammers`. Each check: call `requireAuthFromRequest`, fetch user doc, call `isSoftBanned` ÔÇö if true, return `403 { error: "Your account is restricted from [action]. Reason: [reason]. Contact support if you believe this is an error." }`. Admin and employee role bypass soft ban checks. **Also**: write `getBanSummary(user): { activeBans: UserSoftBan[], expiredBans: UserSoftBan[] }` helper for display in user settings and admin view. `npx tsc --noEmit` Ôćĺ 0 errors. |
| BAN3 | Hard ban enforcement + cascade | M | Ôťů | Depends on BAN1. **Apply hard ban** via new API route `POST /api/admin/users/[id]/hard-ban` (requires `admin:user-bans:write`): (1) Call Firebase Admin `auth.updateUser(uid, { disabled: true })` to block login; (2) Set `isDisabled: true`, `hardBanReason`, `hardBannedAt`, `hardBannedBy` on UserDocument; (3) Cascade: delete all `sessions/{id}` docs where `userId === uid` (revoke active sessions); (4) If user is a seller: set store `status: "suspended"` and bulk-set all their product/auction/preorder `status: "archived"`; (5) Cancel all `bids` where `bidderId === uid` and `status: "active"` Ôćĺ set to `"cancelled"`; (6) Write a `notifications` doc to user: "Your account has been permanently suspended. [reason]. You may appeal by emailing support@letitrip.in." **Lift hard ban** via `POST /api/admin/users/[id]/unban`: calls `auth.updateUser(uid, { disabled: false })`; clears `isDisabled/hardBanReason/hardBannedAt/hardBannedBy`; does NOT auto-restore listings ÔÇö admin manually re-activates those via products page. **Soft ban apply/lift**: `POST /api/admin/users/[id]/soft-ban` (action, reason, expiresAt?); `DELETE /api/admin/users/[id]/soft-ban/[action]`. Notification on apply: "Your account has been restricted from [action]. Reason: [reason]. Expires: [date or 'Never']." `npx tsc --noEmit` Ôćĺ 0 errors. |
| BAN4 | Support ticket API + limit enforcement engine | M | Ôťů | Depends on BAN1. **`POST /api/support/tickets`** (authenticated only ÔÇö no guests): (1) Verify auth (no guest tokens accepted); (2) Check `create_support_tickets` soft ban; (3) Load ticket limits from `siteSettings.platformLimits.maxOpenTicketsPerUser` (default 2) and `siteSettings.platformLimits.maxOrderTicketsPerOrder` (default 1); (4) For `category !== "order_issue"`: call `supportRepository.countActiveTickets(userId)` ÔÇö if Ôëą 2 return `422 { error: "You already have 2 open tickets. Please wait for them to be resolved before opening a new one." }`; (5) For `category === "order_issue"`: validate `orderId` is present; fetch order ÔÇö reject if order `status` is `DELIVERED`, `CANCELLED`, or `REFUNDED` (`400 { error: "Support tickets can only be opened for active orders." }`); call `supportRepository.getActiveOrderTicket(userId, orderId)` ÔÇö if exists return `422 { error: "You already have an open ticket for this order." }`; (6) Check same-category duplication: if an active ticket with the same category and `status: "waiting_on_user"` exists, reject `422 { error: "You have an unanswered question from support for this topic. Please respond to your existing ticket first." }`; (7) Create ticket doc with `status: "open"`, `priority: "normal"`. **`GET /api/support/tickets`** (user's own tickets, paginated). **`POST /api/support/tickets/[id]/messages`** (add message to thread ÔÇö both user and assigned support can use this). **`GET/PATCH /api/admin/support-tickets`** (admin list + status/assignment update, requires `admin:support-tickets:read/write`). All validation server-side, never trusted from client. `npx tsc --noEmit` Ôćĺ 0 errors. |
| BAN5 | Guest checkout block | S | Ôťů | Depends on BAN1. **(1) Checkout API**: `POST /api/checkout/route.ts` ÔÇö add `requireAuthFromRequest(request)` at the very top (before any cart/order logic); if unauthenticated return `401 { error: "Please sign in to complete your purchase." }`. **(2) Cart Ôćĺ Checkout UI flow**: in the cart drawer/page "Proceed to Checkout" button ÔÇö if `user` is null (guest), replace the button with a "Sign in to checkout" CTA that opens the auth modal/redirects to login; pass `redirect=/checkout` as query param so user lands back on checkout post-login. **(3) Checkout page** `src/app/[locale]/checkout/page.tsx` ÔÇö add server-side `getServerSessionUser()` check; if null, `redirect(ROUTES.AUTH.LOGIN + "?redirect=/checkout")`. No other guest flows are affected ÔÇö browsing, wishlists-as-guest, and adding to cart remain available without login. `npx tsc --noEmit` Ôćĺ 0 errors. |
| BAN6 | Admin ban management UI | M | Ôťů | Depends on BAN2, BAN3. **(1) Extend `AdminUserEditorView` SideDrawer** (VA10) to add a "Moderation" tab alongside existing fields: **Hard ban section** ÔÇö `isDisabled` toggle renamed to "Account suspended"; when toggling on: show `hardBanReason` textarea (required); confirm modal "This will disable login, revoke sessions, suspend their store, and cancel active bids. Reason: [reason]."`). **(4) `onUserUnbanned`** (detect `isDisabled` flipping to false): write notification to restored user ("Your account access has been restored."); notify `admin:user-bans:read` employees. All functions use the existing `notifications` collection shape. Use `Promise.all` for batch notification writes. `npx tsc --noEmit` Ôćĺ 0 errors in `functions/`. |

---

## Tier SCAM ÔÇö Scam Awareness System *(low priority)*

> **­čôÉ Layered shape (S14+):**
> - **Constants:** `_internal/shared/features/scams/config.ts` ÔÇö `SCAM_TYPES` (already exists; ensure exported from this path), `SCAM_CATEGORIES`, `SCAM_SEVERITY_LEVELS`.
> - **Types:** `_internal/shared/features/scams/types.ts` ÔÇö `ScamDocument`, `ScamProfile`, `ScamReport`, `ScamType`, `ScamCategory`.
> - **Validation:** `_internal/shared/features/scams/schema.ts` ÔÇö Zod for scam profile create/patch + report submission.
> - **Data layer:** `_internal/server/features/scams/data.ts` ÔÇö `getScamProfile(slug)` (React.cache), `listScams({ filters })`, `listSitemapScams()`.
> - **Business logic:** `_internal/server/features/scams/service.ts` ÔÇö `assertScamRegisterAllowed(uid)`, `acknowledgeScamRegistration(uid)`; errors `ScamProfileNotFoundError`, `ScamReportRateLimitError`.
> - **Actions:** `_internal/server/features/scams/actions.ts` ÔÇö `createScamProfile`, `updateScamProfile`, `submitScamReport`, `verifyScamReport` (`"use server"`; gated by RBAC `scam_moderator` / `trust_and_safety`).
> - **Repository:** existing `scammerRepository` (re-home reference under feature barrel).
> - **Orchestration:** `_internal/server/jobs/handlers/scamNotificationDispatch.ts` (notifies followers/community on new verified profile).
> - **Views:** `AdminScammersView`, `ScamProfilePublicView`, `ScamRegistrationAcknowledgementModal`, FAQ entries (content seed only ÔÇö no view component).
> - **Consumer wiring:** `[locale]/admin/scammers/page.tsx`, `[locale]/scams/[slug]/page.tsx`, `[locale]/scams/page.tsx` (list).
> - **OG + sitemap:** `src/app/[locale]/scams/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx` (1200├Ś630, profile card with masked identifier + scam type badges); `listSitemapScams()` exported and wired into `src/app/sitemap.ts`.
> - **Error handling:** missing profile Ôćĺ `notFound()`; admin-only mutate Ôćĺ 403 with typed error code; report rate-limit Ôćĺ toast.
> - **Verification:** SSR HTML for `/scams/<slug>` contains profile + JSON-LD `Person` markup; `curl -sI .../opengraph-image` Ôćĺ 200 image/png; admin CRUD `tsc` 0/0; viewport sweep + dark-mode repaint.

> **Design intent**: A publicly visible, SEO-optimised scam database that (1) educates the collectibles community about how they get cheated, (2) names known bad actors with evidence, and (3) is mandatory reading for all new registrants. Admin employees verify and publish scammer profiles. The system is deeply integrated with the RBAC tier ÔÇö only `scam_moderator` and `trust_and_safety` employees can verify profiles; any authenticated user can submit a report.
>
> **27 scam types** across 6 categories (defined as `SCAM_TYPES` constant in `appkit/src/features/scams/constants/scam-types.ts`):
>
> | Category | Types |
> |---|---|
> | **Price Manipulation** | `undervaluation` ÔÇö tricks seller into believing item is worth far less ("it's just an old toy"); `fake_price_reference` ÔÇö fake screenshot showing lower price elsewhere; `bait_and_switch` ÔÇö advertises one price, changes after engagement; `condition_misrepresentation` ÔÇö lists mint/sealed/graded, ships damaged/fake |
> | **Social Engineering** | `sympathy_play` ÔÇö impersonates a student/child who "can't afford" market price, guilt-trips seller into discount or deferred payment; `trust_building_fraud` ÔÇö months of small friendly purchases then one large scam; `urgency_pressure` ÔÇö "I'm leaving the city in 1 hour, send now"; `student_impersonation` ÔÇö specific variant: claims to be a broke student collector |
> | **Payment Fraud** | `advance_payment_ghost` ÔÇö takes full advance payment then ghosts; `fake_payment_screenshot` ÔÇö sends photoshopped UPI/PayTM success screenshot; `partial_payment_ghost` ÔÇö pays earnest money, takes delivery, ghosts for rest; `chargeback_fraud` ÔÇö pays via Razorpay/credit card, receives item, disputes with bank; `overpayment_scam` ÔÇö "accidentally" overpays Ôé╣5,000 for Ôé╣500 item, asks for Ôé╣4,500 refund before initial payment clears |
> | **Pre-order & Delivery Fraud** | `preorder_hold` ÔÇö collects deposits from many buyers, holds money for months claiming "delays", eventually refunds only after public noise ÔÇö never had a supplier; `fake_preorder_listing` ÔÇö lists high-demand limited items for preorder with zero supplier relationship; `endless_delay_scam` ÔÇö ships deliberately late (after refund window closes) with vague updates |
> | **Identity & Impersonation** | `seller_impersonation` ÔÇö steals product photos from a reputable seller and runs identical listing at slightly lower price; `platform_impersonation` ÔÇö fake "LetItRip Support" WhatsApp/DM asking for OTP/bank details; `account_takeover_resale` ÔÇö hacks/takes over dormant legitimate seller account to exploit their review history; `fake_escrow` ÔÇö creates a fake "middleman escrow" that is themselves |
> | **Item Authenticity Fraud** | `counterfeit_item` ÔÇö sells replica/bootleg as genuine (fake holographic Pok├ęmon cards, recast Funko Pops, reproduction vintage Hot Wheels); `fake_grading_claim` ÔÇö claims PSA/BGS graded, shows photoshopped certificate; `graded_case_tampering` ÔÇö cracks a legitimate PSA slab, swaps in a fake/lower card, reseals; `sealed_product_repack` ÔÇö opens booster boxes, removes valuable pulls, reseals with hot glue, resells as factory sealed |
> | **Logistics Fraud** | `empty_box_ship` ÔÇö ships an empty box or rocks/newspaper; `fake_tracking_number` ÔÇö generates tracking label but never drops package at courier; `return_swap_fraud` ÔÇö receives genuine item, returns empty box or damaged swap, claims refund |
>
> **Scammer profile document** (`scammers` Firestore collection, prefix `scammer-`): `id`, `slug`, `displayName` (as they presented themselves), `phones: string[]`, `upiIds: string[]`, `emails: string[]`, `socialMedia: { platform: SocialPlatform; handle: string; url?: string }[]`, `scamType: ScamType`, `scamPlatform: ScamPlatform`, `description: string` (rich HTML ÔÇö detailed account of what happened), `amountLost?: number` (paise), `itemInvolved?: string`, `evidence: string[]` (media URLs ÔÇö chat screenshots, payment screenshots, listing photos), `reportedBy: string` (userId), `reportedByAnon: boolean` (if reporter chose to remain anonymous in public view), `status: "pending_review" \| "verified" \| "rejected" \| "removed"`, `verifiedBy?: string`, `verifiedAt?: Timestamp`, `relatedScammerIds: string[]`, `tags: string[]`, `seoSlug: string`, `views: number`, `createdAt: Timestamp`, `updatedAt: Timestamp`. **`ScamPlatform`**: `"letitrip" \| "whatsapp" \| "olx" \| "facebook_marketplace" \| "instagram_dms" \| "telegram" \| "in_person" \| "local_market" \| "other"`. **`SocialPlatform`**: `"instagram" \| "facebook" \| "twitter_x" \| "whatsapp" \| "telegram" \| "youtube" \| "other"`.
>
> **SEO-first design**: every scammer profile page has a unique `/scams/[slug]` route, full `generateMetadata` (name in title, scam type in description, og:image from evidence), FAQ schema JSON-LD, and phone/UPI/email plaintext in the HTML so they are indexed by search engines. The goal: someone searching a phone number or UPI ID finds our page immediately.
>
> **Mandatory registration acknowledgement**: after email verification, new users see a non-skippable scam awareness modal with 5 key facts (one per scam category), a link to `/scams`, and a required checkbox "I have read the scam awareness guide and understand these risks." Tracked as `scamAwarenessAcknowledgedAt?: Timestamp` on `UserDocument`. The modal is shown until acknowledged; after acknowledgement it never appears again.
>
> **Do SCAM1 Ôćĺ SCAM2 Ôćĺ SCAM3 Ôćĺ SCAM4 Ôćĺ SCAM5 Ôćĺ SCAM6 Ôćĺ SCAM7 Ôćĺ SCAM8 in order. SCAM9 (RBAC wiring) should be done alongside RBAC4/RBAC7 when that tier is implemented.**

## Tier EX ÔÇö Extended Homepage Sections

> **Design intent**: Enhancements to existing homepage section types. All changes are backward-compatible. Old section docs without new fields render using existing defaults. Admin builders in AdminSectionsView.tsx expose new config fields. Schema changes go in appkit/src/features/homepage/schemas/firestore.ts; live-stats.ts extended for collection queries. Do EX1 -> EX2 -> EX3 -> EX4 -> EX5 in order.
>
> **EX5 note**: the new collection-cards section type does NOT delete the 8 specialized section types ÔÇö those remain as legacy aliases. Admin can create new sections using the unified type; old sections render via existing components until migrated.

## Tier AX ÔÇö Action System & URL Patterns

> **Design intent**: (1) Eliminate ~200 copy-pasted onClick router.push + toast chains across admin/store/public pages via a typed ACTION constant system with useActionDispatch() hook. (2) Make every admin/store CRUD panel deep-linkable via URL search params (?panel=create / ?panel=edit&id=slug). (3) Standardise sticky form action bars across all FormShell-based forms.
>
> **Implementation order**: AX1 -> AX2 (depends on AX1) -> AX3 (depends on UX1 FormShell).

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| AX1 | Centralized ACTION constants + useActionDispatch hook | M | Ôťů | **Session 90 (2026-05-11) ÔÇö fully done.** Constants: `appkit/src/features/products/constants/action-defs.ts` ÔÇö ACTION_ID/ROW_ACTION_ID/FORM_ACTION_ID/DASHBOARD_QUICK_ACTION_ID + all META maps + preset groups. Hook: `appkit/src/react/hooks/use-action-dispatch.ts` ÔÇö useActionDispatch(options?) returns async dispatch(action) handling NAVIGATE/OPEN_PANEL/TOAST/BULK/COPY. Store: `appkit/src/stores/panel-store.ts` ÔÇö Zustand usePanelStore (panelId, data, openPanel, closePanel, isPanelOpen). Zustand v5 added to appkit deps. Migration: SellerProductsView.tsx handleEdit migrated from router.push to dispatch({ type: "NAVIGATE" }). All exported from client.ts + index.ts. 0 TS errors both repos, appkit build clean. |
| AX2 | Edit/Create URL routing ÔÇö panel auto-open on URL params | M | Ôťů | **Session 92 (2026-05-11) ÔÇö done.** usePanelUrlSync hook (URL ?panel=create/edit&id=xxx); DataTable onRowClick prop; embedded prop on all 7 AdminXxxEditorViews; 8 admin listing views wired with inline SideDrawer + embedded editor; exported from index.ts + client.ts. 0 TS errors both repos. | Depends on AX1. **Pattern**: listing pages read URL search params ?panel=create or ?panel=edit&id={slug}. On mount: if params present -> dispatch(ACTION.OPEN_PANEL(panelId, { id })). On panel onClose/onSuccess -> router.replace(basePath) (removes query params). **usePanelUrlSync(panelId, basePath)** hook (new, appkit/src/hooks/): reads useSearchParams(), on mount calls dispatch if params match, subscribes to panelStore ÔÇö when panel closes, calls router.replace(basePath). **Deep-link format**: /admin/products?panel=create (create panel opens); /admin/products?panel=edit&id=product-abc (edit panel opens pre-loaded). **Wire into**: admin products, auctions, preorders, stores, categories, brands, blog, events, FAQs, coupons (10 admin listing pages) + all store-seller listing pages. **Share**: copy icon in panel header -> ACTION.COPY(window.location.href, "Edit link copied") after URL is updated on open. Add ROUTES.ADMIN.PRODUCT_EDIT(id) etc. helper functions to route-map. npx tsc --noEmit -> 0 errors. |
| AX3 | Sticky form action bars ÔÇö desktop top + mobile bottom | S | Ôťů | **Session 92 (2026-05-11) ÔÇö done.** FormActionBar component (sticky top desktop, sticky bottom mobile, breadcrumbs, dirty-dot, Discard/Preview/Save Draft/Publish); isDirty flag; browser tab title "* " prefix; ConfirmModal on Esc when dirty; wired in FormShell. 0 TS errors both repos. | Depends on UX1 (FormShell). Extends FormShell spec: **Desktop** ÔÇö sticky top bar: breadcrumb trail + resource name + [Preview] [Save Draft] [Publish]. Position: sticky top-[var(--header-height,0px)] z-[var(--appkit-z-dropdown)]. Background: var(--appkit-color-surface) with bottom border. **Mobile** (< md) ÔÇö sticky bottom bar: [Discard] [Save Draft] [Publish]. Position: sticky bottom-0, same z-index. Top bar hidden on mobile (space constraint). **Dirty state**: when any form field changes, set isDirty flag. Browser tab title prepends "* " while dirty. Esc when dirty: show ConfirmModal ("Discard unsaved changes?") before closing. **Toast on action**: Save Draft -> toast "Draft saved" (success). Publish -> toast "Published successfully" (success). Validation error -> toast "Fix the errors above" (error) + scroll to first error field. **FormActionBar** component (new, appkit/src/ui/components/): props { title, breadcrumbs, onSaveDraft, onPublish, onPreview, onDiscard, isDirty, isSubmitting }. Used by FormShell. npx tsc --noEmit -> 0 errors. |

## Tier FI ÔÇö Product Feature Icons & Badges

> **Design intent**: A flexible feature-flagging system for listings. Platform defines standard icons (free shipping, verified seller, condition badges, etc.). Stores and admin can create custom feature icons. Products carry a features: string[] array of feature IDs. Cards and detail pages render small icon badges. Some features are product-type specific (e.g., Auction Winner Badge applies to auctions only). Slug prefix: feature-.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| FI1 | productFeatures schema + repository | S | Ôťů S8 2026-05-11 ÔÇö schema + repo + ProductDocument.features already present; appkit exports wired. | **New file** appkit/src/features/products/schemas/product-features.ts. ProductFeatureDocument: id (slug, prefix feature-), slug, label, description (optional), icon (icon name key from appkit icon set OR SVG path string), iconColor (optional CSS var token key e.g. "--appkit-color-primary"), category ("shipping"/"seller"/"condition"/"platform"/"auction"/"preorder"/"custom"), scope ("platform"/"store"), productTypes (array: "product"/"auction"/"preorder"/"all"), storeId (optional, required if scope=store), isActive (boolean), displayOrder (number), createdAt (Timestamp). Register slug prefix feature- in CLAUDE.md slug table. **Repository** appkit/src/repositories/product-features.repository.ts: list({ scope?, storeId?, productType?, isActive? }), findById(id), create(data), update(id, data), delete(id), listPlatform(), listForStore(storeId). **ProductDocument extension**: add features?: string[] (optional array of feature IDs ÔÇö absent = no features) to appkit/src/features/products/schemas/firestore.ts. Export from appkit. npx tsc --noEmit -> 0 errors. |

## Tier BK ÔÇö Public Bulk Actions

> **Design intent**: Let both authenticated and guest users select multiple products on listing pages and perform bulk actions (compare, wishlist, share). Selection state is ephemeral (in-memory only, not persisted). Guest users can compare and share; auth users additionally add to wishlist. Compare is capped at 4 items. The compare overlay shows items side-by-side (desktop: table; mobile: swipeable cards).
>
> **2026-05-15 migration**: `BulkActionsBar` (old full-width bottom slide-up bar) fully replaced by `BulkActionBar` (inline dropdown + Apply button, renders null when `selectedCount=0`) across every listing page ÔÇö public, admin, and seller. `BulkActionItem.id` replaces legacy `key` field. `useBulkSelection` hook wired on every listing view; manual `Set<string>` state removed. See `appkit/src/ui/components/BulkActionBar.tsx`.

## Tier WA ÔÇö WhatsApp Business Integration *(low priority ÔÇö post-alpha)*

> **­čôÉ Layered shape (S14+ remaining tasks):** WA1ÔÇôWA4 are Ôťů in legacy paths; any new WA work and any WA migration to the new layout follows this shape:
> - **Constants:** `_internal/shared/features/whatsapp/config.ts` ÔÇö Meta Cloud API base URL, batch size (50), version pin.
> - **Types:** `_internal/shared/features/whatsapp/types.ts` ÔÇö `WaBusinessSendInput`, `CatalogSyncProduct`, `CatalogSyncResult`, `PurchaseAnnouncementInput`.
> - **Validation:** `_internal/shared/features/whatsapp/schema.ts` ÔÇö Zod for store WhatsApp settings PUT body.
> - **Data layer:** `_internal/server/features/whatsapp/data.ts` ÔÇö `getWaConfigForStore(storeId)` (decrypted token never leaves server).
> - **Business logic:** `_internal/server/features/whatsapp/service.ts` ÔÇö `assertWaCapability(storeId)` (RBAC `whatsapp_catalog_sync`); errors `WaCapabilityMissingError`, `WaCatalogSyncError`.
> - **Actions:** `_internal/server/features/whatsapp/actions.ts` ÔÇö `updateStoreWaSettings`, `syncStoreCatalog`, `sendOrderAnnouncement` (`"use server"`).
> - **Repository:** extends existing `storeRepository` for `whatsappConfig` block.
> - **Orchestration:** `_internal/server/jobs/handlers/{onOrderCreate.waAnnounce,catalogSyncScheduled}.ts`.
> - **Views:** `StoreWhatsAppSettingsView`, group-share-link button component.
> - **Consumer wiring:** `[locale]/store/whatsapp/page.tsx` (already exists in legacy path; re-wire SSR via data fn).
> - **OG + sitemap:** **N/A**.
> - **Error handling:** capability missing Ôćĺ 403 with admin-contact CTA; sync failure Ôćĺ toast + retry button; token expired Ôćĺ re-auth banner.
> - **Verification:** Meta Cloud API sandbox round-trip; capability gate test (capability removed Ôćĺ 403); `tsc` 0/0.

> **Design intent**: Allow store owners to sync their standard products to their own WhatsApp Business Catalog (per-store Meta credentials). Platform admin receives a WhatsApp message (Meta Cloud API) whenever a new order is placed ÔÇö announcement also sent to the store owner. Group posting is not possible via API; a wa.me share link is provided instead. Full plan in `C:\Users\mohsi\.claude\plans\plan-and-add-support-compressed-snowflake.md`.

## Tier GD ÔÇö In-App Guide Pages *(­čÜź SUPERSEDED by Tier DX 2026-05-12)*

> **­čÜź SUPERSEDED by Tier DX (2026-05-12)** ÔÇö all 22 tasks (GD1ÔÇôGD22) consolidated into the unified docs portal at `docs.letitrip.in`. Mapping:
> - GD1ÔÇôGD6 Ôćĺ DX16ÔÇôDX21 (`docs.letitrip.in/sellers/*`)
> - GD7ÔÇôGD11 Ôćĺ DX11ÔÇôDX15 (`docs.letitrip.in/help/*`)
> - GD12 (capability-gated UX) Ôćĺ DX32 in-app residual (`CapabilityGateView`)
> - GD13ÔÇôGD22 Ôćĺ DX22ÔÇôDX31 (`docs.letitrip.in/employees/*`)
>
> The GD task rows below remain as the **authoritative content-source spec** for the corresponding DX MDX pages ÔÇö port the section content verbatim. Do not mark GD rows Ôťů when implementing DX; track progress on DX rows instead. Three pieces remain in-app because they depend on live user state: DX32 (capability gates), DX33 (personalized onboarding checklist), DX34 (sidebar Help links + footer links).
>
> ~~Original spec preserved below for content reference:~~

> **­čôÉ Layered shape (S14+):** pure RSC content ÔÇö no Firestore reads, no mutations.
> - **Constants:** `_internal/shared/features/guides/config.ts` ÔÇö `GUIDE_SLUGS`, `GUIDE_CATEGORIES`, `GUIDE_AUDIENCES` (admin / store / buyer).
> - **Types:** `_internal/shared/features/guides/types.ts` ÔÇö `GuideEntry`, `GuideCategory`, `GuideSection`.
> - **Validation:** **N/A** (static content).
> - **Data layer:** `_internal/server/features/guides/data.ts` ÔÇö `listGuides({ audience })`, `getGuide(slug)`, `listSitemapGuides()` (all read static module ÔÇö no Firestore).
> - **Business logic:** **N/A** (read-only).
> - **Actions:** **N/A**.
> - **Repository:** **N/A** ÔÇö content lives at `_internal/shared/features/guides/content/<slug>.mdx` (or `.tsx` if richer).
> - **Orchestration:** **N/A**.
> - **Views:** `GuideHubView`, `GuidePageView`, `GuideSidebar` (audience-scoped TOC).
> - **Consumer wiring:** `src/app/[locale]/help/page.tsx` (buyer hub), `src/app/[locale]/help/<slug>/page.tsx`; `src/app/[locale]/admin/guide/<slug>/page.tsx`; `src/app/[locale]/store/guide/<slug>/page.tsx` ÔÇö all pure RSC, capability/permission filtered for admin/store hubs.
> - **OG + sitemap:** per-guide `src/app/[locale]/help/<slug>/opengraph-image.tsx` (1200├Ś630, audience badge + title); `listSitemapGuides()` exported and wired into `src/app/sitemap.ts`.
> - **Error handling:** missing slug Ôćĺ `notFound()`; admin guide accessed without permission Ôćĺ render skeleton with "You don't have access to this guide" notice (do NOT 403, since the index entry should still render).
> - **Verification:** Lighthouse SEO Ôëą 95 per guide; viewport sweep + dark-mode repaint; `tsc` 0/0; `npm run build` succeeds with all new RSC pages compiled.

> **Design intent**: Rich, section-based guide pages embedded in all three dashboards (admin, store, buyer) and the public help center. Unlike the FAQ system (short Q&A answers), guides are long-form reference documents with step-by-step walkthroughs, field-by-field form explanations, status lifecycle diagrams, capability/permission upgrade prompts, and plain-language summaries written for non-technical users. Goal: any user ÔÇö seller, buyer, or internal employee ÔÇö should be able to understand every feature, form, and workflow without leaving the app.
>
> **Three guide surfaces**: (1) **Admin guide** ÔÇö lives at `/admin/guide/*`, accessible to all admin and employee roles; permission-aware (only shows sections the logged-in employee can access). Covers every admin panel and all 18 employee permission groups. (2) **Store guide** ÔÇö lives inside `/store/guide/*`, accessible only to store owners. Covers every seller-facing feature and all 18 store capabilities. (3) **Buyer help center** ÔÇö lives at public `/help/*`, accessible without login. Covers the complete buyer journey.
>
> **Sidebar placement (enforced for all three)**: every guide hub must have a dedicated nav entry in its dashboard sidebar ÔÇö admin: `ADMIN_NAV_GROUPS` Help group (bottom of sidebar); store: `STORE_NAV_GROUPS` Help group; user dashboard: `USER_NAV_GROUPS` Help link pointing to public `/help`. Sidebar entries are wired in GD13 for admin; GD1 already covers store; GD7 covers the user/footer links.
>
> **Content rules**: use only appkit primitives (`Section`, `Container`, `Heading`, `Text`, `Badge`, `Alert`, `Collapsible`, `Stack`, `Row`). No hardcoded hex or breakpoints. All guide content is static (no Firestore reads) ÔÇö these are pre-authored pages, not CMS-driven. Brand name **LetItRip** throughout. Collectibles-niche examples only (Pok├ęmon TCG, Hot Wheels, Beyblades, anime figures).
>
> **Sequence**: GD1ÔÇôGD6 (store guides) and GD7ÔÇôGD11 (buyer guides) are independent. GD12 depends on RBAC8. GD13ÔÇôGD22 (admin guides) depend on RBAC1 for permission-aware rendering but can be built as static pages first and made permission-aware in the same session as RBAC3/RBAC7.

why revoking is preferable to deleting; how to re-enable (set `isDisabled: false` + re-assign permissions). **Section 6 ÔÇö Permission audit best practices**: review employee permissions quarterly; log of who granted what is stored in `users/{uid}/banHistory` subcollection (reused for permission change events). `npx tsc --noEmit` Ôćĺ 0 errors. |
| GD21 | Admin: Analytics Guide | S | ÔĆ│ | **New page** `/admin/guide/analytics`. **New view** `AdminAnalyticsGuideView`. | GD22 | Admin: Trust & Safety Guide ÔÇö bans, scams, support tickets | L | ÔĆ│ | **New page** `/admin/guide/trust`. **New view** `AdminTrustGuideView`. Requires `admin:user-bans:read` or `admin:scammers:read` or `admin:support-tickets:read` or full admin ÔÇö show only the sections the employee has access to. **Section 1 ÔÇö Soft bans vs hard bans**: soft ban = restricts specific actions (`BannedAction` values: `write_reviews`, `write_blog_comments`, `join_events`, `place_bids`, `create_listings`, `send_messages`, `create_support_tickets`, `report_scammers`) while account remains active; hard ban = disables Firebase Auth account, suspends store, cancels bids, revokes sessions ÔÇö nuclear option; when to use each (soft ban: single policy violation; hard ban: fraud, persistent abuse, legal requirement). **Section 2 ÔÇö Applying a soft ban** (step-by-step): open Admin Users Ôćĺ find user Ôćĺ Moderation tab Ôćĺ Add soft ban Ôćĺ select action + reason + optional expiry Ôćĺ Save; user receives notification immediately; ban is enforced server-side on the relevant API route; expired bans are treated as lifted without deletion. **Section 3 ÔÇö Applying a hard ban** (step-by-step + cascade effects): Moderation tab Ôćĺ "Suspend account" toggle Ôćĺ enter reason Ôćĺ Confirm; cascade: Auth disabled Ôćĺ sessions deleted Ôćĺ store suspended Ôćĺ active bids cancelled Ôćĺ notification sent to user; how to lift (Unban button ÔÇö does NOT auto-restore listings). **Section 4 ÔÇö Ban appeal process**: user contacts support via email (not ticket ÔÇö `create_support_tickets` is soft-banned); `trust_and_safety` employee reviews evidence; lift via Admin Users Ôćĺ Moderation tab. **Section 5 ÔÇö Scam report workflow** (for `scam_moderator` and `trust_and_safety`): report comes in with `status: "pending_review"`; admin reviews identity + evidence + incident description; "Verify & Publish" (sets `status: "verified"`, notifies reporter) vs "Reject" (notifies reporter with reason); editing a verified profile (updating fields does NOT reset status); contest handling ÔÇö if accused contests, review `contests` subcollection Ôćĺ "Uphold" (update profile + mark contest resolved) vs "Dismiss"; when to "Remove" a verified profile (false identity, legal takedown). **Section 6 ÔÇö Support ticket workflow** (for `customer_support` and `support_agent`): ticket states (open Ôćĺ in_progress Ôćĺ waiting_on_user Ôćĺ resolved Ôćĺ closed); who can do what (read: all support roles; write/reply: read/write; assign: assign permission; close: close permission); SLA guidelines (first response within 4 hours for high/urgent; 24 hours for normal; 48 hours for low); escalation path (escalate priority + notify all `admin:support-tickets:read` employees); internal notes field (never visible to user ÔÇö use for escalation context, account observations). **Section 7 ÔÇö Trust metrics** (`Alert variant="info"`): how `helpfulCount` on reviews works; how `views` on scammer profiles is used (trending scam types); how to interpret `reportedByAnon` (reporter chose anonymity ÔÇö do not expose their identity even internally). `npx tsc --noEmit` Ôćĺ 0 errors. |

## Sessions SB1ÔÇôSB10 ÔÇö Bundle & Prize Draw Listings + Event Raffle System
> Added: 2026-05-11

> **­čôÉ Layered shape (mandatory for every SB row):** every SB-series task above the `Status` column must, when implemented, conform to the shape below. Existing single-line `Notes` columns predate the SSR rearch and stay as-is for reference; the layered breakdown below is the **authoritative spec** for implementation.
>
> **Constants:** `_internal/shared/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/config.ts` ÔÇö `BUNDLE_MAX_ITEMS`, `BUNDLE_MAX_PER_USER_DEFAULT`, `PRIZE_DRAW_MIN_ITEMS`, `PRIZE_DRAW_MAX_ITEMS`, `PRIZE_DRAW_REVEAL_DEADLINE_DAYS_DEFAULT`, `EVENT_RAFFLE_TYPES`, `SPIN_PRIZE_MAX`.
>
> **Types:** `_internal/shared/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/types.ts` ÔÇö `BundleDocument`, `BundleItem`, `PrizeDrawDocument`, `PrizeDrawItem`, `EventRaffleConfig`, `SpinPrize`, `ListingType` (extended union: `"standard" | "auction" | "pre-order" | "prize-draw" | "bundle"`).
>
> **Validation:** `_internal/shared/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/schema.ts` ÔÇö Zod discriminated union on `listingType`; `prizeDrawItemSchema` (min 3, max 16); `bundleItemSchema` (min 2 child products); `spinPrizeSchema` (weighted; sum of weights normalised server-side).
>
> **Data layer:** `_internal/server/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/data.ts` ÔÇö `getBundle(slug)`, `listBundles({ filters, page, pageSize })`, `getPrizeDraw(slug)`, `listPrizeDraws()`, `getEventRaffle(eventId)`, `listSitemapBundles()`, `listSitemapPrizeDraws()`, `listSitemapEventRaffles()`. All reads use `React.cache`.
>
> **Business logic:** `_internal/server/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/service.ts` ÔÇö `assertBundleStock(bundleId, qty)`, `assertBundlePerUserLimit(uid, bundleId)`, `assertPrizeDrawNotExpired(drawId)`, `assertPrizeDrawCapacity(drawId)`, `assertRafflePoolNonEmpty(eventId)`, `assertSpinNotUsed(uid, eventId)`. Domain errors: `BundleStockError`, `BundleNonRefundableConsentMissingError`, `BundlePerUserLimitError`, `PrizeDrawExpiredError`, `PrizeDrawCapacityError`, `RafflePoolExhaustedError`, `SpinAlreadyUsedError`.
>
> **Actions:** `_internal/server/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/actions.ts` ÔÇö `createBundle`, `updateBundle`, `deleteBundle`, `purchaseBundle`, `revealPrize`, `triggerEventRaffle`, `assignSpinPrize` (`"use server"`).
>
> **Repository:** new `bundlesRepository`, `prizeDrawsRepository`, `eventRafflesRepository` in `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/<x>/repository.ts` ÔÇö extending `BaseRepository` (override `createWithId` per recurrent root-cause #9). Migration script for `listingType` discriminator move (SB1-A) replaces the legacy `isAuction`/`isPreOrder` boolean pair across all collections.
>
> **Orchestration:** `_internal/server/jobs/handlers/{onBundlePurchase,prizeDrawAutoRefund,prizeDrawReveal,eventRaffleSpin,eventRaffleWinnerNotify,bundleStockSync}.ts` ÔÇö registered via `bindToFirebase()` per Arch-S6.
>
> **Views:** `_internal/client/features/{bundles,prize-draws,event-raffles}/<X>View.tsx` ÔÇö `BundleDetailView`, `BundlesListView`, `BundleItemsPicker`, `BundleForm`, `NonRefundableConsentModal`, `PrizeDrawDetailView`, `PrizeDrawItemsEditor`, `PrizeRevealModal`, `Collage`, `EventRaffleWinnerView`, `SpinWheelView`.
>
> **Consumer wiring:** `src/app/[locale]/bundles/page.tsx`, `src/app/[locale]/bundles/[slug]/page.tsx`, `src/app/[locale]/prize-draws/page.tsx`, `src/app/[locale]/prize-draws/[slug]/page.tsx`, `src/app/[locale]/events/[slug]/winner/page.tsx`, plus store/admin sub-pages ÔÇö every page pre-fetches via the data fn and passes `initialBundle` / `initialPrizeDraw` / `initialEventRaffle`.
>
> **OG + sitemap:** `src/app/[locale]/bundles/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx`, `src/app/[locale]/prize-draws/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx`, `src/app/[locale]/events/[slug]/winner/opengraph-image.tsx`. Sitemap data fns wired into `src/app/sitemap.ts`.
>
> **Error handling:** stock-out Ôćĺ inline form error + cart-line removal; expired prize draw Ôćĺ 410 page; raffle pool empty Ôćĺ admin notification + buyer 404; non-refundable consent missing Ôćĺ checkout-blocking modal; per-user limit exceeded Ôćĺ toast + `Add to wishlist` CTA.
>
> **Verification:** SSR HTML for bundle/prize-draw/raffle detail contains title + price + items; `auto-refund` job dry-run; `crypto.randomInt`-based reveal/spin reproducible only with stored seed; viewport sweep xs Ôćĺ 2xl + dark-mode repaint on every new page; `tsc` 0/0; `audit-violations` exit 0.

| SB4-H | Prize Reveal API route ÔÇö crypto.randomInt + pool exhaustion | Ôťů | **Done S7-PrizeDraws-prep3 2026-05-13.** New `src/app/api/prize-draws/[id]/reveal/route.ts`. POST body `{ orderId }`; auth required. Pre-tx existence + ownership + payment + window + deadline checks (fail-fast). Transactional reveal: re-reads product + order under lock, re-checks idempotency, filters `unwonItems`, picks via `crypto.randomInt(0, unwonItems.length)`, flips `items[pickIndex].isWon = true` on the product doc, writes `order.prizeWon`. Pool-exhausted path marks the order REFUNDED + `isNonRefundable: false` + returns `{ refunded: true, reason: "pool_exhausted" }` (covers SB8-C). Idempotent: re-posting after success returns the same prize without re-rolling. Public response never echoes the prize pool's `isWon` map. ~~Original spec:~~ **New file:** `src/app/api/prize-draws/[id]/reveal/route.ts`. POST `{ orderId }`. Auth required. Steps: verify order ownership + paid; verify `order.prizeDrawProductId === productId`; idempotency check (`order.prizeWon === null`); verify `prizeRevealStatus === "open"` + within window + before deadline; filter `unwonItems`; if empty Ôćĺ refund + return `{ refunded: true, reason: "pool_exhausted" }`; else `crypto.randomInt(0, unwonItems.length)` Ôćĺ pick winner; update order.prizeWon; set prizeDrawItem.isWon=true; return `{ prizeWon: { itemNumber, title, images, estimatedValue } }`. `npx tsc --noEmit` Ôćĺ 0 errors. |
| SB4-I | PrizeRevealModal component | Ôťů | **Done S7-PrizeDraws-prep3 2026-05-13.** New `appkit/src/features/products/components/PrizeRevealModal.tsx`. Modal owns four phases (`idle` / `revealing` / `won` / `refunded` / `error`). On "Reveal my prize" CTA it calls `/api/prize-draws/[id]/reveal` (or a `onReveal` slot for custom envs), then runs a 3.2-second decelerating highlight cycle (`CYCLE_INTERVAL_FAST` 80 ms Ôćĺ `CYCLE_INTERVAL_SLOW` 360 ms) across the collage using `highlightItemNumber`, finally landing on the winning tile. After animation: winner card with image + estimated value. Pool-exhausted + already-revealed branches handled. Persistent fairness disclaimer with the `prizeGithubFileUrl` callout addresses the "show that it looks real but disclaim that it's pure RNG" requirement raised in-session. Cleans timers on unmount/close. ~~Original spec:~~ **New file:** `appkit/src/features/products/components/PrizeRevealModal.tsx`. Triggered on order detail page when reveal conditions met. Countdown to deadline. "Reveal My Prize" button Ôćĺ API call. CSS card-flip animation on success. Shows won item: number, title, images, estimated value, RNG Source Code link. If already revealed: show won item directly without re-draw. `npx tsc --noEmit` Ôćĺ 0 errors. |

### SB11 ÔÇö Homepage Sections: Bundles, Prize Draws & Event Raffles

> **Why here:** Bundles and prize draws are new listing types (SB1ÔÇôSB4). They need dedicated homepage section types so the CMS admin can surface them on the homepage ÔÇö the same way standard products, auctions, and pre-orders already have section types. Event raffles (SB9) also get a section type so live raffle events can be promoted on the homepage. All three section types are **additive** ÔÇö no existing section types change. Seed docs are disabled-by-default so they don't render before the underlying data exists. SB11 depends on the schemas from SB1-A (listingType), SB1-E (BundleDocument), SB4 (PrizeDrawDocument shape), and SB9-A/SB9-B (EventType raffle). SB11 can be planned and scaffolded independently; it needs SB3/SB4/SB9 data to actually render anything.
>
> **Relationship to SB5-D:** SB5-D planned seeding `section-featured-bundles` and `section-prize-draws` as "reuse existing section types". Those types don't exist yet. SB11-A defines them. SB11-G handles the three new disabled seed docs. SB5-D should be updated to only seed `section-brand-hot-wheels` and `section-brand-pokemon` (which reuse existing `brand-spotlight` or `brands` section types).
>
> **Session assignment:** SB11 fits into Session 93 alongside EX1ÔÇôEX5/YT1 (extended homepage sections). All three new section components are async RSC and query their own collections ÔÇö no architecture change needed.

|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| SB11-A | Schema ÔÇö 3 new HomepageSectionType values + config interfaces | M | Ôťů | S7 2026-05-11. `"featured-bundles" \| "prize-draws" \| "event-raffles"` added to `SectionType` union. `FeaturedBundlesSectionConfig`, `PrizeDrawsSectionConfig`, `EventRafflesSectionConfig` interfaces added. `SectionConfig` discriminated union extended. `DEFAULT_SECTION_ORDER` updated (20/21/22). 0 TSC errors. |
| SB11-B | `FeaturedBundlesSection` component | L | Ôťů | S7 2026-05-11. Async RSC at `appkit/src/features/bundles/components/FeaturedBundlesSection.tsx`. Uses HTML wrappers (Section/Container/Stack/Text/Heading) + zinc tokens ÔÇö no hex, no breakpoints. Future: bundle data fetch + card grid wired when `bundles` collection ships. |

## Tier LR ÔÇö Lint Refactor: Raw HTML Element Migration *(stamped 2026-05-12)*

> Added 2026-05-12. `lir/no-raw-html-elements` + `lir/no-raw-media-elements` errored across 36 legacy files (192 errors total) blocking the `npm run check` gate. Each file got a top-of-file `/* eslint-disable lir/no-raw-html-elements, lir/no-raw-media-elements -- LR1: legacy raw HTML, migration tracked in crud-tracker.md Tier LR */` stamp so the gate exits 0 without losing the migration backlog. **Every disabled file is a row in this tier ÔÇö closing a row removes the disable.**
>
> **Migration recipe per file:** (1) replace `<h1>`/`<h2>`/`<h3>` with `<Heading level={N}>`; `<p>` with `<Text>`; `<span>` with `<Span>` or `<Text inline>`; `<button>` with `<Button variant=ÔÇŽ>`; `<a>` with `<TextLink>` or `<Link>` (from `@/i18n/navigation`); `<img>` with `<Image>` (next/image) or `<MediaImage>`; `<video>` with `<MediaVideo>`. (2) Remove the file-top disable. (3) Run `npm run check:lint -- <file>` to confirm zero errors. (4) Re-flow the file through `npm run check` end-to-end.

| # | File | Error count | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-------------|--------|-------|
| LR1-01 | `src/components/dev/SeedPanel.tsx` | 26 | ÔĆ│ | Dev tooling; heavy raw `<div>`/`<span>` use. Big file (>1200 LOC) ÔÇö split the migration into Basics / Accordion / per-collection card sections. |

### LR2 ÔÇö Appkit lint backlog *(separate from letitrip src)*

> Discovered 2026-05-12. `npm run check`'s `check:lint` step only lints `src/**` (letitrip). Running `npx eslint src/**/*.{ts,tsx}` inside `appkit/` surfaces **404 errors** that the gate doesn't see today. Adding appkit lint to the gate now would block all forward work; this row tracks the cleanup so it gets done.

| # | Rule | Count | Status | Migration approach |
|---|------|-------|--------|--------------------|
| LR2-A | `@typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any` | 228 | ÔĆ│ | Each `any` is a type-debt entry. Sweep by feature (e.g. `appkit/src/features/products/**`, then `auctions/**`). Per file: replace with concrete type, `unknown`, or generic. Some inevitable in adapter layers ÔÇö leave `// eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any` with a `LR2-A: <reason>` comment. |
| LR2-B | `@typescript-eslint/no-unused-vars` | 150 | ÔĆ│ | Mostly unused params + leftover imports from refactors. `--fix` handles many; the rest are intentional (destructured `_ignored`) and need `_` prefix. |
| LR2-C | `@typescript-eslint/no-empty-object-type` | 21 | ÔĆ│ | `interface Foo {}` placeholders left over from incremental design. Either give them a body or replace with `type Foo = Record<string, never>`. |
| LR2-D | Other (`prefer-const`, malformed JSDoc) | 5 | ÔĆ│ | One-off cleanups. |

**Activation plan**: once LR2-A/B/C land, wire appkit eslint into the root `npm run check:lint` so future regressions block the gate.

## Tier OG ÔÇö OpenGraph Image Coverage *(post-alpha; backlog audit)*

> **Design intent:** every public detail page (one resource at one URL) ships an `opengraph-image.tsx` so social shares render rich previews. As of 2026-05-12, 7 detail families have OG images (products, auctions, pre-orders, stores, brands, blog, events). This tier closes the gap on existing routes; OG tasks for **new** resources (bundles, prize-draws, scams, guides, etc.) live with their own tier and are not duplicated here.
>
> **­čôÉ Layered shape (S14+):** OG tasks are pure consumer-wiring + verification ÔÇö most layers **N/A**. *Data layer*: reuse the existing per-feature `data.ts` getter (`getCategoryBySlug`, `faqRepository.getBySlug`, etc.). *Consumer wiring*: the new `opengraph-image.tsx` file itself, edge runtime, `ImageResponse` 1200├Ś630. *OG + sitemap*: this row IS the OG task; sitemap entries already exist on the listing data fns. *Error handling*: missing resource Ôćĺ fall back to default OG image at `src/app/opengraph-image.tsx`. *Verification*: `curl -sI http://localhost:3000/<route>/opengraph-image` Ôćĺ `200 image/png` + visual check in Twitter/Facebook debugger; `npm run build` includes the new edge route.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| OG1 | OG image for category detail page | S | Ôťů | **Done S6 2026-05-13.** `appkit/src/_internal/server/features/categories/og.tsx` ÔÇö two-layer renderer (`renderCategoryOg` mapping CategoryDocument Ôćĺ OG data; `renderCategoryOgImage` pure JSX primitive) ÔÇö cover image background from `display.coverImage`, name + 140-char description + product-count chip from `metrics.totalItemCount`. `src/app/[locale]/categories/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx` thin page shim. Node runtime per OG-FIX1. Pagination wrappers (`categories/sort/[sortKey]/page/[page]`, `categories/[slug]/[tab]/sort/[sortKey]/page/[page]`) are exempt in `verify-og-coverage.mjs` ÔÇö OG belongs on the canonical detail. |
| OG2 | `faq/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx` | S | ÔŁî | **N/A ÔÇö S6 2026-05-13.** Verified routes: `/faq` (single list page), `/faqs/[category]` (category listing). No `/faq/[slug]` detail route exists. FAQs aren't deep-linked as individual share targets. Category-listing OG is captured under the `OG-coverage-followup` row below. |

| OG5 | Audit script: `appkit/scripts/verify-og-coverage.mjs` | M | Ôťů | **Done S6 2026-05-13.** Walks `src/app/[locale]/**/page.tsx`, identifies public dynamic-leaf routes ([slug]/[id]/[storeSlug]/etc.), checks for a sibling `opengraph-image.tsx`. Follow-up row added below to drive the baseline to 0. |
| OG-coverage-followup | Per-feature OG renderers for the 5 baseline gaps | M | ÔĆ│ | New baseline tracked in `appkit/scripts/verify-og-coverage.mjs:OG_KNOWN_GAPS`. Drive count to 0 by shipping renderers for: `bundles/[slug]` (bundle title + storeName + price + N-item chip), `faqs/[category]` (category name + LetItRip wordmark), `reviews/[id]` (rating stars + product title ÔÇö needs `_internal/server/features/reviews/og.tsx`), `scams/[id]` (scam type badge + first 200 chars of body ÔÇö surface-level alert tone), `sellers/[id]` (sellers index doesn't have a [id] route in the codebase; verify the page exists or remove from gap list). Each follows the brand/store pattern. Verification: `npm run audit:og-coverage` Ôćĺ "baseline gaps: 0 known". |
| OG-FIX1 | Edge-runtime build break ÔÇö `node:fs` / `crypto` in OG routes | M | Ôťů S23-follow-up 2026-05-12 ÔÇö applied fix path (a): dropped `export const runtime = "edge"` from all 9 OG routes via the new `scripts/strip-og-edge.mjs` helper. Routes now default to Node runtime; the 2 edge-runtime warnings from `appkit/dist/features/auth/{token-store,consent-otp}.js` (via /api/stores reviews + /api/checkout + checkout.actions) also disappeared. `npm run build` exits 0; zero warnings. Long-term path (b) ÔÇö thin `_internal/server/og/` getters ÔÇö can revisit when cold-start latency becomes a problem. Original notes: | **Production blocker.** Verified S23 2026-05-12: `npm run build` fails at `Collecting page data` with `Failed to load external module node:fs: Native module not found: node:fs` originating from `/[locale]/blog/[slug]/opengraph-image` (and likely all sibling edge OG routes). Root cause: OG routes declare `runtime = "edge"` but import from `@mohasinac/appkit/server`, whose chain pulls in `appkit/dist/features/auth/token-store.js` (`import crypto from "crypto"`) and `consent-otp.js` (`import { createHmac, randomInt } from "crypto"`). Build also surfaces 2 edge-runtime warnings from the same chain via `/api/stores/[storeSlug]/reviews/route.ts`, `/api/checkout/route.ts`, `src/actions/checkout.actions.ts` (callers not declared edge so they're warnings, not errors). **Fix paths to evaluate**: (a) switch OG routes off edge to Node runtime ÔÇö simplest, costs cold-start latency; (b) add per-feature thin OG data getters in `appkit/src/_internal/server/og/` that import only the bare minimum (no auth/checkout chain) ÔÇö best long-term; (c) carve `appkit/server` into smaller edge-safe entry points. Last touched in `22a4f3c5e refactor(og): tighten consumer shims` ÔÇö predates this session. Verification: `npm run build` exits 0 + every `/<route>/opengraph-image` returns `200 image/png` against `curl -sI`. |
| OG-FIX2 | `outputFileTracingIncludes` moved out of `experimental` | XS | Ôťů S23-follow-up 2026-05-12 ÔÇö `appkit/src/configs/next.ts` `defineNextConfig` now reads `outputFileTracingIncludes` as a top-level override key, merges the firebase-admin/lib/database forcing as the default, and emits it at the top of the returned config (not under `experimental`). `NextConfigOverride` interface gained the typed field. `npm run build` no longer prints the "Unrecognized key" warning. Original notes: | Build warning: `Unrecognized key(s) in object: 'outputFileTracingIncludes' at "experimental"`. Next 16 moved this option to the top-level config. One-line move in `next.config.js` (or in `defineNextConfig` inside `appkit/src/configs/next.ts` if that's where the wrapper sets it). Non-blocking but noisy in every build. |
| DEV-1 | `watch:css` produces degraded `dist/tailwind-utilities.css` | S | ÔĆ│ | Discovered S23 2026-05-12 via the Stop hook: when `npm run dev` is left running, appkit's `watch:css` overwrites `dist/tailwind-utilities.css` with a build missing the `md:` / `lg:` breakpoint utilities (Tailwind scans `dist/` before TSC has finished emitting, so the `min-width:768px` / `min-width:1024px` class strings aren't seen and get purged). `verify-css-build` then fails on next `npm run check`. One-command recovery: `npm --prefix ./appkit run build`. **Fix paths**: (a) point `watch:css` at `src/**` (not `dist/**`), (b) gate `watch:css` on a first-pass TSC completion via a small wrapper, or (c) restore the build CSS on dev shutdown via the `killTree` hook in `scripts/dev-next.mjs`. Tracked so the next audit failure has a one-link explanation. |
| DEV-2 | Dev heap cap probe: 1024 MB OOMs, 2048 MB stable | S | Ôťů S23-followup 2026-05-12 ÔÇö new `scripts/probe-dev-heap-cap.mjs` boots `next dev --webpack` at incremental caps (1024 Ôćĺ 1536 Ôćĺ 2048 ÔÇŽ) with light load (6 routes rotated every 4 s for 2 min/cap), distinguishing natural OOM from deliberate-kill. Results on this codebase: 1024 MB OOMs (peak RSS 1457 MB), 1536 MB survives (peak RSS 1887 MB), 2048 MB over-permissive (V8 grows to fill). Per "minimum no-crash + 512 MB headroom" rule Ôćĺ **2048 MB**. Applied to `package.json` `dev:only` NODE_OPTIONS, `scripts/dev-next.mjs` HOBBY_LIMITS.MEMORY_MB, `scripts/next-memory-forensics.js` HEAP_CAP_MB default. CLAUDE.md Rule #6 + `memory/project_vercel_hobby_limits.md` rewritten for Fluid Compute Standard reality (2 GB per-function, 8 GB build machine). |
| DEV-3 | Vercel `.next/` upload OOM blocked deploy | XS | Ôťů S23-followup 2026-05-12 ÔÇö first `vercel --prod` attempt blew up the CLI with `Array buffer allocation failed` because 41 GB of `.next/` build cache + leaked heap snapshots sat in the upload tree. `.vercelignore` now excludes `.next/`, `memory-forensics-*`, `*.heapsnapshot`, `probe-results.json`. Subsequent upload was 2.2 MB. |
| DEV-4 | Vercel build broken on `firebase-functions/v2/*` (Module not found) | M | Ôťů S23-followup 2026-05-12 ÔÇö appkit's `server-entry.ts` re-exported `bindToFirebase` + 22 job handlers from `_internal/server/jobs/index`, which imports `firebase-functions/v2/{https,scheduler,firestore}`. Local webpack dev externalised those via `defineNextConfig`'s `externals` callback; **Vercel's prod build uses Turbopack** which won't externalize an uninstalled package. Two failed published versions chased this (2.5.0 had the issue; 2.5.1 added `firebase-functions` to `FIREBASE_EXTERNAL_PACKAGES` but Turbopack ignored it). **Fix: carved `@mohasinac/appkit/jobs` subpath** in 2.6.0 ÔÇö bindToFirebase + handler re-exports moved there, server-entry.ts dropped the block. `functions/src/index.ts` updated to import from `@mohasinac/appkit/jobs`. Letitrip's Next bundle never reaches `firebase-functions` now. |
| DEV-5 | Prod deploy live on `www.letitrip.in` | XS | Ôťů S23-followup 2026-05-12 ÔÇö after DEV-3 + DEV-4 fixes, `vercel deploy --prod --yes` succeeded. Deployment `letitrip-pmnjd95r1-mohasin-ahamed-chinnapattans-projects.vercel.app` aliased to `https://www.letitrip.in`; `curl -sI` returns `HTTP/1.1 200 OK` + Next 16 font + CSS preload chain. SB3 (Bundle Listings) + all S23 work is now in production. |

## Tier EMG ÔÇö Emerging Patterns *(holding bay for code/copy mentions without tasks)*

> **Process note:** whenever a session notices a feature, payment method, integration, or content type that is referenced in code or copy but has no implementation task, **append a row here in the same session ÔÇö do not wait for triage**. EMG is the holding bay until a feature graduates into its own tier or scheduled session. Re-scan triggers: any new mention surfaced by `grep` for keywords (`EMI`, `installment`, `gift card`, `loyalty`, `live chat`, `affiliate`, `referral`, `crypto`, `subscription`, `B2B`, `wholesale`); any FAQ or seed-copy mention of a flow with no code path; any partial implementation in `letitrip.in/functions/src/` not surfaced in the public app. Each row carries the full layered shape (or explicit **N/A**) so it is implementation-ready when scheduled.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| EMG1 | EMI / installment payment at checkout | L | ­čÄ» | **Triage 2026-05-12 (S45):** **ready-to-graduate.** Full layered shape exists in this row + Razorpay supports it via existing webhook + `_internal/shared/features/payments/` would be a new sub-tree (no conflicts). When scheduled, lift this row out of EMG into a new **Tier PAY** (Payments Extensions) or extend **Tier V** at the Versatility level. Recommend pairing with EMG3 (gift cards) so payments work is a single multi-session arc instead of two staggered ones. **Discovery:** `appkit/src/seed/faq-seed-data.ts` line 571 ("UPI, COD, EMI"); `src/components/dev/SeedPanel.tsx:874` ("Payment Methods FAQs (UPI, COD, EMI)"). **Verified 2026-05-12:** zero implementation across `appkit/src/` and `src/` (grep `EMI\|installment` Ôćĺ only seed copy). Razorpay supports EMI via `payment_capture` config + EMI plans; Bajaj Finserv is a viable alt provider. **­čôÉ Layered shape:** *Constants:* `_internal/shared/features/payments/config.ts` ÔÇö `EMI_MIN_CART_VALUE_PAISE`, `EMI_PROVIDERS`, `EMI_TENURES_MONTHS`. *Types:* `_internal/shared/features/payments/types.ts` ÔÇö `EmiPlan`, `EmiOption`, `PaymentMethodWithEmi`. *Validation:* `_internal/shared/features/payments/schema.ts` ÔÇö Zod for EMI selection at checkout. *Data layer:* `_internal/server/features/payments/data.ts` ÔÇö `getEmiPlansForAmount(amountPaise)`. *Business logic:* `_internal/server/features/payments/service.ts` ÔÇö `assertEmiEligible(cartTotal)`; error `EmiNotEligibleError`. *Actions:* extend `createOrder` to accept EMI plan; new `recordEmiSelection`. *Repository:* extend `ordersRepository` `paymentMethod` enum to include `EMI_*`. *Orchestration:* `_internal/server/jobs/handlers/onEmiOrderCreate.ts` (server-side polling for EMI capture confirmation); reuse Razorpay webhook for capture event. *Views:* `EmiOptionsList` (checkout panel), `EmiBadge` on product card ("EMI from Ôé╣X/mo"). *Consumer wiring:* `CheckoutRouteClient.tsx` payment-method picker; `ProductDetailPageView` EMI badge. *OG + sitemap:* **N/A**. *Error handling:* ineligible cart Ôćĺ option hidden + tooltip; provider failure Ôćĺ fallback to standard payment + toast. *Verification:* Razorpay test EMI flow end-to-end (test card); product card badge renders only when `price Ôëą EMI_MIN_CART_VALUE_PAISE`; `tsc` 0/0. |

## Tier PL ÔÇö Listing Quality Polish Pass (`S-polish-pass`)

> Full plan + architectural rules: `~/.claude/plans/plan-to-find-and-polished-aho.md`. Slot after S11. Every task in this tier must respect two foundational rules: (1) **no in-memory filtering** ÔÇö all list ops at query layer; (2) **readable URL params** ÔÇö `sort=newest&type=auction&page=2` in the browser, translated to Sieve DSL internally.

## Tier RA ÔÇö Retrofit Audit (SSR-Design Conformance) *(audits Ôťů tasks against the layered template)*

> One audit row per existing tier that has Ôťů rows. Each audit walks the tier and confirms each feature against the SSR-design checklist below. Audit rows are **read-only**; any gap flips the original Ôťů to ÔÜá´ŞĆ and adds a concrete fix row under the original tier (one commit = one work unit).
>
> **Checklist applied per feature:**
> ```
> Ôľí TEMPLATE     _internal/server/features/<feature>/ has data.ts / adapters.ts / actions.ts / index.ts (where applicable)
> Ôľí CACHE        Every data fn shared between page+generateMetadata is wrapped in React.cache
> Ôľí SHIM         Every consumer page.tsx ÔëĄ30 lines (no Firestore query in page)
> Ôľí INITIAL      Every detail page passes initialX to its view component (no double-fetch)
> Ôľí OG           Every detail route has opengraph-image.tsx as ÔëĄ30-line shim Ôćĺ appkit renderer
> Ôľí NO-HARDCODE  No "LetItRip" / "letitrip.in" / currency / route strings inside _internal/
> Ôľí OPTS         Every public appkit function takes opts?: XOptions
> Ôľí SLOTS        Every appkit view accepts at least one renderXxx slot
> Ôľí EXPORTS      Server fns in server-entry.ts; client fns in client-entry.ts; no firebase-admin reachable from client-entry
> Ôľí NO-DUP       Run the Duplication Decision Framework on every cross-tier overlap
> ```

| # | Task | Status | Notes |
|---|------|--------|-------|
| RA-Tier1 | Retrofit audit ÔÇö Tier 1 Rich Text System | ÔĆ│ | |
| RA-Tier2 | Retrofit audit ÔÇö Tier 2 Product Custom Fields & Detail Sections | ÔĆ│ | |

### Ôćĺ Tier AK ÔÇö *Phase 2: DI seams for swappable features*

> Every feature below gets an `I<Feature>Provider` interface in `appkit/src/contracts/`, a default impl, and registration via `appkit/src/contracts/registry.ts`. Consumer registers its own impl at boot to replace any of them without forking appkit.

| # | Task | Status | Notes |
|---|------|--------|-------|
| AK2-checkout-di | Add `ICheckoutProvider` contract: `createOrder(cart, address, payment)`, `validateCart(cart)`, `getSteps()`. Refactor `CheckoutView` to consume provider via `useCheckoutProvider()`. Keep current logic as `DefaultCheckoutProvider`. | ÔĆ│ | Flagship example. Cart stays in appkit untouched; checkout becomes consumer-replaceable. |
| AK2-cart-di | Add `ICartProvider` contract: `getCart()`, `addItem()`, `removeItem()`, `merge(guest, user)`, `clear()`. Cart hooks (`useCart`, `useAddToCart`) consume via provider. Default = current localStorage + Firestore impl. | ÔĆ│ | Lets consumer swap to Redis/server-cart without touching UI. |
| AK2-notification-di | Add `INotificationProvider` contract: `notify({type, title, body, userId, entityId})`. Default = Firestore `notifications` collection. Consumer can register FCM/email/webhook impl. | ÔĆ│ | Currently hardcoded to `notificationsRepository` everywhere. |
| AK2-media-upload-di | Add `IMediaUploadProvider` contract: `requestSignedUrl(ctx)`, `confirmUpload(slug)`, `abortUpload(slug)`. Default = current Firebase Storage signed-URL flow. | ÔĆ│ | Lets consumer swap to S3/Cloudinary/Bunny. `generateMediaFilename(ctx)` stays in appkit. |
| AK2-address-di | Add `IAddressValidationProvider` contract: `validate(address)`, `normalize(address)`, `geocode?(address)`. Default = pincode-only India validation. | ÔĆ│ | Currently inlined in `AddressForm`. |
| AK2-search-pluggable | `ISearchProvider` already exists in `contracts/search.ts` ÔÇö audit `SearchView` to confirm it consumes via provider not direct repo calls. Fix gaps. | ÔĆ│ | Audit + retrofit. |
| AK2-copilot-classify | Audit `features/copilot/` ÔÇö decide pure-client vs. provider-backed. If provider: add `ICopilotProvider`. | ÔĆ│ | Cross-links `X-copilot-classify`. |
| AK2-registry-doc | Document the full provider registry in `appkit/README.md` ÔÇö every `I*Provider`, default impl, how to register a custom one. Include the 6-level Override Hierarchy. | ÔĆ│ | Cross-links `IX-override-doc` + `IX-appkit-docs`. |

### Ôćĺ Tier AK ÔÇö *Phase 3: SOLID + design-principles sweep*

| # | Task | Status | Notes |
|---|------|--------|-------|
| AK3-srp-audit | **SRP** ÔÇö flag any `_internal/server/features/<f>/data.ts` doing mutations (belongs in `actions.ts`) or `actions.ts` doing reads (belongs in `data.ts`). | ÔĆ│ | Punch-list output; each gap Ôćĺ fix row under owning tier. |
| AK3-ocp-slots | **OCP** ÔÇö every appkit view export accepts at least one `renderXxx` slot prop. Gaps become rows. | ÔĆ│ | Sister to lint rule `X-slots-lint`. |
| AK3-lsp-repo | **LSP** ÔÇö any subclass overriding `BaseRepository` methods in a way that breaks the parent contract (e.g. `createWithId` bypass ÔÇö recurrent pattern #9). | ÔĆ│ | Generate rows for each violator. |
| AK3-isp-contracts | **ISP** ÔÇö split fat `I*Provider` contracts (>6 methods) into role-specific sub-contracts (e.g. `ICheckoutValidator` + `ICheckoutOrchestrator` + `ICheckoutPayment`). | ÔĆ│ | Apply to new AK2 contracts before they fossilize. |
| AK3-dip-direct-repo | **DIP** ÔÇö every appkit component/hook importing a concrete repository instead of a provider. Each Ôćĺ fix row. | ÔĆ│ | Structural enforcer for AK2. |
| AK3-opts-everywhere | Backfill `opts?: XOptions` on every appkit public function lacking it. Codified by `X-opts-lint`. | ÔĆ│ | |
| AK3-dry-duplication | **DRY** ÔÇö run Duplication Decision Framework (CLAUDE.md) on every cross-feature overlap surfaced during AK1. | ÔĆ│ | Cross-links `IX-DUP-AUDIT`. |
| AK3-yagni-prune | **YAGNI** ÔÇö flag any contract method / slot prop / opts field with **zero callers**. Delete or document a near-term consumer. | ÔĆ│ | |
| AK3-demeter | **Law of Demeter** ÔÇö flag chains like `user.profile.settings.theme.color` deeper than 2 hops in appkit code. Introduce intermediate accessors. | ÔĆ│ | |
| AK3-composition | **Composition over Inheritance** ÔÇö audit `appkit/src/repositories/` + `_internal/server/features/*/` class hierarchies. Anything Ôëą3 levels deep Ôćĺ `mixin(BaseRepo, [WithPII, WithAudit, WithCache])`. | ÔĆ│ | |
| AK3-tell-dont-ask | **Tell-Don't-Ask** ÔÇö flag controllers reading state then calling back (`if (cart.isEmpty()) cart.addItem(x)` Ôćĺ `cart.addIfEmpty(x)`). | ÔĆ│ | Surfaces missing intent methods on providers. |

## Tier AP ÔÇö Architectural Patterns (beyond DI) *(post-beta)*

> GoF / DDD / CQRS patterns either already informal in the codebase or that would materially simplify upcoming work. Each row formalizes one pattern with a clear seam.

| # | Task | Status | Notes |
|---|------|--------|-------|
| AP1-strategy | **Strategy** ÔÇö extract pluggable algorithms: `IPricingStrategy` (regular/auction/pre-order/bundle/prize-draw), `IDiscountStrategy` (percentage/fixed/free-shipping/BOGO), `IShippingRateStrategy` (flat/weight/Shiprocket). Default strategies via registry. | ÔĆ│ | Aligns with SB1 listingType migration. |
| AP2-adapter | **Adapter** ÔÇö every `_internal/server/features/<f>/adapters.ts` must export `toClientX(doc)` + `fromClientX(payload)` symmetric pair. Codify naming + signature; lint rule `lir/require-adapter-pair`. | ÔĆ│ | Already partially in place. |
| AP3-facade | **Facade** ÔÇö document that appkit barrels (`index.ts`, `client.ts`, `server.ts`) ARE facades. Nothing outside appkit may reach into `appkit/src/features/**` directly. Lint via `lir/no-deep-appkit-import` (extend existing `lir/no-deep-barrel-import`). | ÔĆ│ | |
| AP4-repository-decorator | **Decorator** ÔÇö replace ad-hoc `BaseRepository` overrides (PII encryption, audit, caching) with composable `withPii(repo)` / `withAudit(repo)` / `withCache(repo)` decorators. Solves `createWithId` bypass class (recurrent #9). | ÔĆ│ | Pairs with `AK3-composition`. Each decorator one file in `appkit/src/repositories/decorators/`. |
| AP5-observer-eventbus | **Observer / Event Bus** ÔÇö `appkit/src/events/` with typed channels: `orderPlaced`, `bidWon`, `productViewed`, `userBanned`. Replaces cross-feature direct chains (order Ôćĺ notification Ôćĺ email). | ÔĆ│ | Default in-process bus; consumer can bridge to pub/sub (FCM, Cloud Tasks). |
| AP6-command-action | **Command** ÔÇö every `"use server"` action follows `{ input: ZodSchema, handler: (input, ctx) => Result, name: string }` shape so they can be queued, retried, audited, replayed. Retrofit one feature at a time. | ÔĆ│ | Foundation for offline-queue + audit log. |
| AP7-cqrs-formalize | **CQRS-lite** ÔÇö codify the existing `data.ts` (queries, `cache()`-wrapped) vs. `actions.ts` (commands) split. Lint rule `lir/no-cross-cqrs-call`. | ÔĆ│ | Sister to `AK3-srp-audit`. |
| AP8-state-machine | **State Machine** ÔÇö formalize lifecycles for order (PENDINGÔćĺPROCESSINGÔćĺSHIPPEDÔćĺDELIVEREDÔćĺREFUNDED), auction (DRAFTÔćĺLIVEÔćĺENDEDÔćĺSETTLED), pre-order (TAKING_ORDERSÔćĺAWAITING_STOCKÔćĺFULFILLINGÔćĺCLOSED), ban (NONEÔćĺSOFTÔćĺHARD), event-entry (PENDINGÔćĺCONFIRMEDÔćĺCANCELLEDÔćĺWAITLISTED). Use lightweight custom FSM or `xstate`. | ÔĆ│ | Replaces scattered `if (status === "X" && newStatus === "Y") allow`. |
| AP9-specification | **Specification** ÔÇö composable Firestore filters: `new ActiveListingsSpec().and(new InCategorySpec(slug)).and(new PriceBetweenSpec(lo, hi))`. Existing sieve is partial impl. | ÔĆ│ | Bridges sieve params (f/s/p/ps/q) to typed predicates. |
| AP10-builder-order | **Builder** ÔÇö `new OrderBuilder().forBuyer(uid).fromCart(cart).withAddress(addr).withCoupon(code).withPaymentMethod(razorpay).build()`. Replaces the current 60-line `createOrder()`. Validation at `build()`. | ÔĆ│ | Used inside `DefaultCheckoutProvider`. |
| AP11-chain-of-resp | **Chain of Responsibility** ÔÇö checkout pipeline: validateCart Ôćĺ applyDiscounts Ôćĺ computeShipping Ôćĺ computeTax Ôćĺ reserveInventory Ôćĺ createPayment Ôćĺ persistOrder Ôćĺ notify. Each link independently testable, registrable, replaceable. | ÔĆ│ | Pairs with AP1 (strategies) + AP6 (commands). |
| AP12-null-object | **Null Object** ÔÇö every `I*Provider` ships a `NoOpXProvider` default so consumers opt out without registering. Remove `?.` chains in callers. | ÔĆ│ | E.g. `NoOpLoggerProvider`, `NoOpNotificationProvider`. |
| AP13-template-method | **Template Method** ÔÇö `BaseRepository` already uses this. Audit + document hook points (`beforeCreate`, `afterCreate`, `beforeUpdate`) so subclasses don't bypass via direct field writes. Pair with AP4 decorators. | ÔĆ│ | |
| AP14-memento-draft | **Memento** ÔÇö formalize draft-save / undo for admin forms (product editor, blog editor, carousel slide builder). One `useDraft(key, snapshot)` hook in appkit. | ÔĆ│ | Each form currently rolls its own localStorage save. |
| AP15-composite-sections | **Composite** ÔÇö homepage sections + carousel + product custom sections are composite trees. Document `ISectionRenderer` contract so new section types plug in without touching `HomepageRenderer` switch. | ÔĆ│ | Replaces the 21-section-type switch. Open/Closed for sections. |
| AP16-principles-doc | Add `appkit/docs/architecture.md` ÔÇö one page per pattern with when to use, when NOT, code example, anti-example, related rules. Index from `appkit/README.md`. | ÔĆ│ | Onboarding artifact. |
