## Tier LP ÔÇö Lint Plugin Migration *(post-beta)*

> Migrate audit scripts into custom `lir/*` rules so there is one source of truth. `verify-css-build.mjs` stays as a script (post-build artifact check). `npm run check:audits` becomes `eslint --rule "lir/audit-*:error" .` after LP1 lands.

### Ôćĺ Tier LP ÔÇö *Phase 1: audit scripts Ôćĺ rules*

| # | Task | Status | Notes |
|---|------|--------|-------|
| LP1-audit-violations | Migrate `appkit/scripts/audit-violations.mjs` Ôćĺ `lir/no-internal-boundary-cross` rule. Enforces `_internal/{client,shared,server}` cross-import bans currently in `appkit/.eslintrc.json` + script. | ÔĆ│ | Delete script after rule lands + `package.json` `check:audits` updated. |
| LP1-verify-entries | Migrate `appkit/scripts/verify-entries.mjs` Ôćĺ `lir/no-firebase-admin-in-client-entry` rule. Walks import graph from `appkit/src/client.ts` / `client-entry.ts`. | ÔĆ│ | Already partly covered by `lir/no-firebase-admin-outside-backend`; this is the entry-graph variant. |
| LP1-audit-ssr | Migrate `scripts/audit-ssr-in-appkit.mjs` Ôćĺ 4 rules: `lir/enforce-ssr-shim-size` (ÔëĄ30 line page.tsx), `lir/enforce-ssr-sidecar` (data.ts/adapters.ts present), `lir/no-hardcoded-branding-in-internal`, `lir/no-fat-og-image` (ÔëĄ40 line opengraph-image.tsx). | ÔĆ│ | Baseline of 8 root violations becomes `warn` for grandfathered files; new files `error`. Cross-links `X-audit-baseline`. |
| LP1-verify-css-keep | Keep `appkit/scripts/verify-css-build.mjs` as-is (post-build artifact check; not lintable). | ÔĆ│ | Marker row documenting the decision. |

### Ôćĺ Tier LP ÔÇö *Phase 2: new rules from CLAUDE.md anti-patterns*

| # | Task | Status | Notes |
|---|------|--------|-------|
| LP2-listing-type | `lir/no-isauction-isPreorder-boolean` ÔÇö flag any read/write of `isAuction` / `isPreOrder` on a product. Use `isAuctionListing(p)` / `normalizeListingType(p)`. Codifies SB1-G Phase 4 (recurrent #1). | ÔĆ│ | Medium. Property-access + object-key + import-name checks. |
| LP2-no-raw-hex | `lir/no-raw-hex-color` ÔÇö flag `#[0-9a-fA-F]{3,8}` in `style={}` props and `*.css` outside variable defs. Use `var(--appkit-color-*)`. | ÔĆ│ | Medium. |
| LP2-no-z-arbitrary | `lir/no-arbitrary-z-index` ÔÇö flag `z-[N]` in className strings. Use `var(--appkit-z-*)`. | ÔĆ│ | Easy. |
| LP2-no-inline-nav | `lir/no-inline-nav-groups` ÔÇö flag inline definition of `*_NAV_GROUPS` or sidebar nav arrays in layout files. Import from `@/constants/navigation`. | ÔĆ│ | Medium. |
| LP2-no-import-side-css | `lir/no-css-at-import-from-node-modules` ÔÇö flag `@import "@mohasinac/*"` in `globals.css`. Forces JS `import "pkg/styles"` in `layout.tsx`. Codifies recurrent #10. | ÔĆ│ | Easy. CSS-AST rule. |
| LP2-routes-strict | `lir/no-hardcoded-route` enhancement ÔÇö extend to cover `redirect()`, `permanentRedirect()`, `Link href={\`/x/${id}\`}`, fetch URLs. | ÔĆ│ | Enhances existing rule. |
| LP2-media-filename | `lir/require-generate-media-filename` ÔÇö flag string literals matching `firebasestorage.googleapis.com` written to Firestore docs. Use `generateMediaFilename(ctx)` + `/media/<slug>` proxy. | ÔĆ│ | Medium. |
| LP2-no-bare-fetch-firestore | `lir/no-direct-firestore-write` ÔÇö flag `setDoc`/`updateDoc`/`addDoc` outside `appkit/src/repositories/` + `_internal/server/features/*/actions.ts`. | ÔĆ│ | Enhances `lir/no-direct-firestore-query`. |
| LP2-opts-suffix | `lir/require-opts-param` (codifies `X-opts-lint`) ÔÇö flag any export from appkit facades whose last parameter is not `opts?:` and has Ôëą1 parameter. | ÔĆ│ | Hard. Public-export crawl. |
| LP2-render-slot | `lir/require-render-slot-prop` (codifies `X-slots-lint`) ÔÇö flag any appkit view-shell export whose props don't include at least one `render*` prop. | ÔĆ│ | Hard. Component-prop type check. |
| LP2-firebase-admin-static | `lir/no-static-firebase-admin-import` ÔÇö flag top-level `import` of `firebase-admin/*` outside `appkit/src/server.ts` + `_internal/server/**` + `repositories/**`. Codifies Turbopack client-bundle trap. | ÔĆ│ | Medium. |
| LP2-sideEffects-flag | `lir/require-sideeffects-false` ÔÇö package.json rule on `appkit/package.json`: `"sideEffects": false` must remain. Without it Turbopack bundles firebase-admin chain. | ÔĆ│ | Easy. JSON rule. |
